  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_12c39b7a-fd89-490d-83d0-db9443357d9a'
      });

<span id="freeTextContainer5335644010129453149">Trez “Latimer” doesn’t really exist. And not just because the identity was created so that a Shadow could function in the underbelly of the human world. He’s never </span>
  <span id="freeText5335644010129453149" style="display:none">Trez “Latimer” doesn’t really exist. And not just because the identity was created so that a Shadow could function in the underbelly of the human world. Sold by his parents to the Queen of the S’Hsibe as a child, Trez escaped the Territory and has been a pimp and an enforcer in Caldwell, NY for years- all the while on the run from a destiny of sexual servitude. He’s never had anyone he could totally rely on... except for his brother, iAm.<br /><br />iAm’s sole goal has always been to keep his brother from self-destructing- and he knows he’s failed. It’s not until the Chosen Serena enters Trez’s life that the male begins to turn things around... but by then it’s too late. The pledge to mate the Queen’s daughter comes due and there is nowhere to run, nowhere to hide, and no negotiating.<br /><br />Trapped between his heart and a fate he never volunteered for, Trez must decide whether to endanger himself and others- or forever leave behind the female he’s in love with. But then an unimaginable tragedy strikes and changes everything. Staring out over an emotional abyss, Trez must find a reason to go on or risk losing himself and his soul forever. And iAm, in the name of brotherly love, is faced with making the ultimate sacrifice...</span>
  <a data-text-id="5335644010129453149" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<span class='communityAnswererName'>

<span class='communityAnswerText'>
<span class="expandableContainer"><span class="truncatedContent">Well I could see it on Starz since they did Spartacus and that was basically blood, guts and sex. Including frontal's of both genders so they obviousl<a class="jsShow showAction" href="#">…more</a></span><span class="fullContent">Well I could see it on Starz since they did Spartacus and that was basically blood, guts and sex. Including frontal's of both genders so they obviously are willing to show the human body. <br /><br />However I have noticed that when I see a movie first I enjoy both but prefer the movie because it presets my mind to what the movie portrayed and the opposite when I read the book first, I tend to not hate but definitely not love the movie. I saw Twilight first and then read the books, 50 shades I read the book first. True blood and Dexter I have only watched the series. I am scared to read the books. The opposite of Cedar Cove series I have only read the series and am hesitant to watch the series. However if Starz did this then I know the hot scenes would not be downplayed. <a class="jsHide hideAction" href="#">(less)</a></span></span>
</span>

<div id="review_1242268318" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1242268318" />
    <a title="Mandi Schreiner" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2704703-mandi-schreiner"><img alt="Mandi Schreiner" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1368979996p2/2704703.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1242268318?book_show_action=true">Mar 31, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mandi Schreiner" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mandi Schreiner" href="/user/show/2704703-mandi-schreiner">Mandi Schreiner</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2704703-mandi-schreiner?shelf=pnr">pnr</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1242268318" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13474873458386777632">We all know I love me some JR Ward. I have a freaking information page that is very out of date but devoted to her. I loooooooove her books. They are cracky fun. They have 500 different plot lines in every one, use ridiculous slang but they are my brothers.<br/><br/>The Shadows came out yesterday. I wasn’t that excited about reading it because Trez and iAm haven’t excited me in the past – but some peeps on Twitter said crazy things happened, so I plopped my butt down and read it. And honestly I started to</span>
  <span id="freeText13474873458386777632" style="display:none">We all know I love me some JR Ward. I have a freaking information page that is very out of date but devoted to her. I loooooooove her books. They are cracky fun. They have 500 different plot lines in every one, use ridiculous slang but they are my brothers.<br /><br />The Shadows came out yesterday. I wasn’t that excited about reading it because Trez and iAm haven’t excited me in the past – but some peeps on Twitter said crazy things happened, so I plopped my butt down and read it. And honestly I started to really get into the story. But then I started seeing all these tweets about a Goodreads post JR Ward (Link contains spoilers) had made with lots of spoilers – so I turned off Twitter and read the book.<br /><br />It’s bullshit. I’ll put the rest under a spoiler tag. It’s VERY spoilery below so please do not click if you have do not want to be spoiled. You have been warned.<br /><br /> <br /><br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<br /><br />SO – this book is 571 pages. About 500 of those featureTrez and Selena. They fall in love. It’s very romantic. I sometimes have a hard time with Ward heroines but I liked Selena a lot. I liked her in the previous book too. She is a chosen, but she is fierce and sexy and likes adventure andadreline. But she is also sick, with a rare disorder that attacks some of the chosen. It’s been fatal in the past, eventually locking up their bones until they die.This goes on for 500 pages – Trez and her living each day to the fullest, allowing Selena to experience things and do everything romantic, while everyone else scrabbles for a cure.Except then she dies.<br />T<br />he heroine of the book, dies. Like dies – and then they burn her body. There is no Jane ghost floating around. There is no miracle like Mary received. She didn’t get sexual healing like No’One/Autumn. She is just plain dead.<br /><br />This is a romance book, right????<br /><br />The golden rule of a romance book is – there is a happily ever after at the end for the main couple. Even a “happy for now” will work. But you see you need that “happy” part. And don’t tell me Trez gazing into the night sky is happy. Trez is now in deep mourning over the death of his bonded one. So…how is this happy? I don’t give a crap that iAm has someone, his romance barely had the page time Trez and Selena’s did. His romance was wayyyy in the background and kind of forced and insta-lust if you ask me. He was not the main character of this book. Trez and Selena were – and she dies.<br /><br />Sorry JR Ward. I don’t care. This is NOT a romance book. I’m sorry if your characters “made” you do this<br /><br /><i>But, as I said, I’m stuck doing what I’m told- so last summer, when Trez and Selena’s outlining process froze early on me, I wasn’t sure what to make of it.</i><br /><br />I don’t care if you didn’t choose this. Because you could have chosen to write it a different way.<br /><br /><i>I don’t “choose” things. I don’t get to pick who ends up with whom, or what happens. I appreciate from the outside how it must appear, that the author is some how “in control,” but that is simply not my experience.<br /><br />I didn’t want Selena to die. I can assure folks that the LAST thing I wanted to do was spend four months writing a book that put me right back into the head space I’d been in losing Jonah. Some of the scenes in THE SHADOWS made me cry so hard, I couldn’t see the dayum computer screen. I hated editing it. I <br />hated copyedits. I hated galleys.</i><br /><br />(<a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.goodreads.com/author_blog_posts/8124484-the-shadows-spoilers-spoilers?page=1">https://www.goodreads.com/author_blog...</a>)<br /><br />I would never want to tell a writer how to write a book. The author and their book have such an intimate relationship. BUT – I’m going to say, don’t kill the hero or the heroine. You don’t get that choice. You want to kill off Selena? Don’t let him bond with her, kill her off in chapter one, and then let Trez fall in love somehow with his actual mate. We let that slide with Wellsie. We didn’t have a Tohr and Wellsie book, so we could just let that slide. But this? Nope. You don’t give us 600 pages of romance, just to kill the heroine. Nope.<br /><br />When we read a romance book, sometimes we are really tested. Horrible things have happened to countless heroes and heroines. Sometimes like Selena, they are fighting a horrible physical disease, sometimes they are abused, sometimes they have to endure tragic things. And the romance reader is sobbing or angry right along with them – but we have trust that the author will give his or her characters a happy ever after by the end of the book. Put us through hell – make us cry, make us rant, make us angry – but make us believe at the end of true love. You broke that trust.<br /><br />This isn’t the end of the world – I realize this is a book and not real life. But enough crap happens in our real lives – I want a happy ever after damn it. And The Shadows does not have one. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></span>
  <a data-text-id="13474873458386777632" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_902368240" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/902368240" />
    <a title="Christy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11284813-christy"><img alt="Christy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1594293998p2/11284813.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/902368240?book_show_action=true">Apr 05, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christy" href="/user/show/11284813-christy">Christy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer902368240" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4830218313067285118"><b>5 stars!</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%204/be2a684c-e2e2-468c-8595-82e0e4164992_zps4c3fad55.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396766888i/9184990.jpg' alt=' photo be2a684c-e2e2-468c-8595-82e0e4164992_zps4c3fad55.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Oh. My. God. THE FEELS. I cried in Z’s book. I cried in Rhage’s book. Those two books were by far the most emotional books for me when it comes to the BDB. But this book? This book made me bawl. There were just a few scenes and situations that I could not control the tears. Did I love it as much as some of the other books in this series? No. I can’t say I did. Some of the earlier ones (Rhage, V, Z) plus Qhuinn and Blay’s book will always be my favorites. But I still think JR Ward has</span>
  <span id="freeText4830218313067285118" style="display:none"><b>5 stars!</b><br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%204/be2a684c-e2e2-468c-8595-82e0e4164992_zps4c3fad55.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396766888i/9184990.jpg" alt=" photo be2a684c-e2e2-468c-8595-82e0e4164992_zps4c3fad55.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Oh. My. God. THE FEELS. I cried in Z’s book. I cried in Rhage’s book. Those two books were by far the most emotional books for me when it comes to the BDB. But this book? This book made me bawl. There were just a few scenes and situations that I could not control the tears. Did I love it as much as some of the other books in this series? No. I can’t say I did. Some of the earlier ones (Rhage, V, Z) plus Qhuinn and Blay’s book will always be my favorites. But I still think JR Ward has an incredible mind, is a crazy talented author and story teller, and I still feel that <i>The Shadows</i> was more than worthy of it’s 5 star rating. <br><br><i>The Shadows</i> primarily focuses on brothers Trez and iAm, although many secondary characters play a large part as well. Trez and iAm are not brothers in the sense that they're in the brotherhood, but they are twin brothers from a tribe called the H’sibe. We got to know them in Rhev’s book and then they were in <i>The King</i> quite a bit as well. In <i>The King</i> we see Trez’s feelings for the Chosen Selena grow. We also find out an interesting tid-bit. That iAm is a <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[virgin <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. I don’t want to rehash their stories. If you’ve read the series then you know what’s going on with them, and if you haven’t it would be too complicated to explain and riddled with spoilers. So I’ll just talk a bit about each of these boys…<br><br><b>Trez</b>. I was more excited to read about iAm then I was Trez when I started this book. I’m going to begin with that. By the end? Trez 100% won me over. His love, his devotion, his heart… I loved everything about him. I loved the romantic side that came out. I didn’t think he had it in him. But as much as I loved it, his was the story that broke me.<br><i>
  <blockquote> “You know what you just proved?”<br>“What?” <br>“That somebody can say ‘I love you’ without speaking.”</blockquote>
</i><br> <b>iAm</b> couldn’t be more different than Trez if he tried. iAm’s always been a great male. A male with standards, who’s self sacrificing and would do anything for the one person in the world he loves more than anyone. His brother. iAm proves just how much he would do for Trez in this book. These brother’s will always hold a special place in my heart. And I am so ecstatic that someone who deserved it got some damn happy in this story! <i>
  <blockquote> “You and I were written in the stars… </blockquote>
</i><br><br>Now I can’t write a review on this book without mentioning my man VISHOUS. I wish he was in this one more, but I’m happy with what I got. And even happier that Ward gave him a <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[tongue ring!!!! <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> Seriously. Love it. <br><br>We’ve already learned that the next story in the BDB will be The Beast. It will be Rhage’s book. I love the idea of going back to the original brothers. And with the way things were set up in <i>The Shadows</i> for Rhage, I think his book will be amazing. I’m excited to see where things go from here. Even though I’m happy about Rhage, I was DYING for an XCOR book. When she finally writes Xcor and Layla’s story… I just have a feeling it will be epic. We’ve been waiting so long. <br><br><i>The Black Dagger Brotherhood</i> will is and will always be one of my favorite series ever. I can’t get enough of these characters and their stories. I’ve been lucky enough to see JR Ward in person twice. This second time was even better than the first. Here are a few pics from event-<br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%207/3c601164-e2ff-412e-9e34-e801cd7eff0a_zpsdgkidc3c.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1428213001i/14389027.jpg" alt=" photo 3c601164-e2ff-412e-9e34-e801cd7eff0a_zpsdgkidc3c.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1230370771?book_show_action=true">Mar 17, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="UniquelyMoi ~ BlithelyBookish" class="user" itemprop="url" name="UniquelyMoi ~ BlithelyBookish" href="/user/show/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish">UniquelyMoi ~ BlithelyBookish</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=series-black-dagger-brotherhood-war">series-black-dagger-brotherhood-war</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=vampires">vampires</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=must-read-series">must-read-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=must-read-author">must-read-author</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=own-have-read">own-have-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=2015-reads">2015-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=author-jr-ward-jessica-bird">author-jr-ward-jessica-bird</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=shadows">shadows</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=not-happily-ever-after">not-happily-ever-after</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=rice-krispies-should-stfu">rice-krispies-should-stfu</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1230370771" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15652837766298055815"><br/><i>Profanities removed and spoilers hidden! Sheesh!</i><br/><br/><b>All bets are off…</b><br/><br/>I have such incredibly mixed feelings about this book, and I’m not sure I’ll ever get them sorted out. Sometimes a story will gut me, and <i>The Shadows</i> did just that. In truth, I don’t remember a time I cried myself to sleep over a book – but I did this time. It was at moments laugh out loud funny, window fogging steamy, sweetly romantic, and profoundly tragic. <br/><br/>I always say that an author should write a story the way that story comes</span>
  <span id="freeText15652837766298055815" style="display:none"><br /><i>Profanities removed and spoilers hidden! Sheesh!</i><br /><br /><b>All bets are off…</b><br /><br />I have such incredibly mixed feelings about this book, and I’m not sure I’ll ever get them sorted out. Sometimes a story will gut me, and <i>The Shadows</i> did just that. In truth, I don’t remember a time I cried myself to sleep over a book – but I did this time. It was at moments laugh out loud funny, window fogging steamy, sweetly romantic, and profoundly tragic. <br /><br />I always say that an author should write a story the way that story comes to him or her, and I stand by that. However, that doesn’t always mean I’ll like the story they felt compelled to tell. Well, the story as The WARDen felt compelled to tell was done so, brilliantly, but this is one of those times when I did <i>not</i> like the story itself. This is not how the <i>Black Dagger Brotherhood</i> series started out, and not since Phury and Cormia’s book have I felt so cheated out of a <i>happly ever after!</i> <br /><br /><b>Blurb…</b><br /><br />Two brothers bound by more than blood fight to change a brutal destiny in the heart-wrenching new novel of the Black Dagger Brotherhood by #1 New York Times bestselling author J. R. Ward.<br /><br />Trez “Latimer” doesn’t really exist. And not just because the identity was created so that a Shadow could function in the underbelly of the human world. Sold by his parents to the Queen of the S’Hsibe as a child, Trez escaped the Territory and has been a pimp and an enforcer in Caldwell, NY for years- all the while on the run from a destiny of sexual servitude. He’s never had anyone he could totally rely on... except for his brother, iAm.<br /><br />iAm’s sole goal has always been to keep his brother from self-destructing- and he knows he’s failed. It’s not until the Chosen Serena enters Trez’s life that the male begins to turn things around... but by then it’s too late. The pledge to mate the Queen’s daughter comes due and there is nowhere to run, nowhere to hide, and no negotiating.<br /><br />Trapped between his heart and a fate he never volunteered for, Trez must decide whether to endanger himself and others- or forever leave behind the female he’s in love with. But then an unimaginable tragedy strikes and changes everything. Staring out over an emotional abyss, Trez must find a reason to go on or risk losing himself and his soul forever. And iAm, in the name of brotherly love, is faced with making the ultimate sacrifice...<br /><br /><b>My thoughts…</b><br /><br />The first 60ish% of the story was amazing. I loved every bit of it and had been thinking, “THIS is the way it should be! THIS is what made me fall in love with the Brotherhood so many years ago!!” Rhage’s one-liners, Lassiter’s eccentric, fallen self, V and Jane’s quickie in the clinic, and Manny and Rhage’s trip to Caldie, everything read like the original books and I was thrilled, and captivated, was falling in love with my Boys all over again! I was basking in all that Caldwell happiness… until <i>it</i> happened and I was devastated.<br /><br />In a blog post explaining why things went the way they did, The WARDen said that if she tries to write a story any other way than the way she sees it, it shuts down. Goes blank. She either tells it the way it comes to her, or it can’t be told. I get where she's coming from, and honestly, as I kept reading late into the night because I needed a miracle…something to fix the unfixable, even as Trez <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[was up on that pyre, <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> I waited. Needing something, <i>any</i>thing to make this right. At the same time, I knew if <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ she pulled a rabbit out of her hat and presto'd the happy ending for Trez and Selena, I would have been disappointed and still miffed that Wellsie died and Jane is Dr. Ghost, MD.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> On one hand, I gotta hand it to her; she stayed true to her Rice Krispies and made it real. On the other hand... it became painfully clear to me that <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ when I'm reading to escape and waiting for the <i>happily ever after</i> that’s going to give me hope that true love exists and can overcome any obstacle… I don't want real. <i>Real. Effing. Sucks!</i> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />And, if <i>this</i> truly is the way <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Trez and Selena’s  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> HEA was meant to play out, it should have played out in a different series, in a different world. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ A world where no one expects <i>happily ever afters… </i> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>The bottom line…</b><br /><br />In the real world things can be horrific and unfair and brutally tragic, which is why I read romance - I want to escape the reality that can be ugly when loved ones pass from our lives. This book is not <i>true</i> romance - not the kind I've come to look forward to from this author. Sure, <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[iAm and the Princess got hooked up,  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> but if that’s supposed to make me feel better, it's a failure of <i>EPIC proportions! </i> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Their HEA sucked. They got the shaft in the <i>happily ever after</i> department and it in no way made up for or eased Trez and Selena’s debacle.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> Am I ready to throw in the BDB Towel? Nope! I’m too invested in the Brothers to turn my back now, but as I said, all bets are off. This book scared the hell out of me because the <i>Black Dagger Brotherhood</i> is no longer a series I can count on to make me forget the real world, if only for a little while. I will always be on guard, always wondering who will be offered up as a sacrifice to the all powerful Rice Krispies next.<br /><br />And <i>that</i> is every bit as heartbreaking as <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Trez and Selena’s <i>happily ever after.</i> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Rating Breakdown:</b><br /><br />Everything excluding the HEA: 5 stars!<br />What has to be the worse HEA ever: 1 star!<br />Overall rating: 2.5 stars rounded to 3 because I can't bring myself to give my Boys less and, besides, none of this mess is their fault...</span>
  <a data-text-id="15652837766298055815" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1243178049" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1243178049" />
    <a title="Jen Davis" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4669344-jen-davis"><img alt="Jen Davis" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1548427639p2/4669344.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1243178049?book_show_action=true">Apr 01, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jen Davis" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jen Davis" href="/user/show/4669344-jen-davis">Jen Davis</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1243178049" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12503333796031080214">If you have managed to make it this far without any spoilers on this book, I congratulate you. There is a reason people are talking about it. Even in the broadest strokes, it's impossible for me not to convey that things go really wrong here. That doesn't mean everyone hated <i>The Shadows</i>. To the contrary, it's got its fair share of 5 star reviews floating around. You'll find readers who love rolling around in the kind of misery only "true love" can precipitate. You'll find others who find beauty </span>
  <span id="freeText12503333796031080214" style="display:none">If you have managed to make it this far without any spoilers on this book, I congratulate you. There is a reason people are talking about it. Even in the broadest strokes, it's impossible for me not to convey that things go really wrong here. That doesn't mean everyone hated <i>The Shadows</i>. To the contrary, it's got its fair share of 5 star reviews floating around. You'll find readers who love rolling around in the kind of misery only "true love" can precipitate. You'll find others who find beauty in despair. And there are still others who feel like JR Ward could rub dog shit around on a piece of white paper and call it art. I fall into none of those categories.<br /><br />To explain how this book is a failure for me, I am going to have to tell you why. I'm not going to spoil every single thing about it, but I am going to talk about the big twist at the end that has split the reading community. Here is your last chance to look away.<br /><br />JR Ward kills the heroine. She is still dead when the book is over and she is not coming back to life. They burned her corpse and sent her off into the Fade. It's the forever kind of dead. And for that, I say JR Ward has broken her covenant with readers. Romance books are supposed to end with a working relationship between the hero and heroine. There is supposed to be happiness there. One isn't supposed to be dead while the other is left a shadow of himself. No pun intended there. I'm too mad.<br /><br />I've actually seen other people claim that these books aren't romance; that they are more urban fantasy. To that, I call bullshit. Yes, Ward has broadened the scope of the series to multiple POVs (too many) but each book follows a core romance. Remember how much it sucked when she killed Wellsie? And she was a secondary character. This is so much worse, and honestly, has about a quarter of the emotional impact. I didn't cry. I wasn't even tempted to cry. I was too annoyed. The move was so very wrong that it pulled me out of the story entirely, just wondering WTF? Meanwhile, we've got iAm percolating a very second-string romance with a ridiculously predictable outcome, and that is supposed to be satisfying? IT'S NOT.<br /><br />I can't even blame the ending as the only problem in the book. Rhage is prominently featured here, which some readers may be excited about. But I swear, he acts like he is losing his marbles. This plot thread recurs over and over and then it is totally dropped with no explanation. It made the character look like he had a personality disorder and then it had no impact on the plot. (And don't get me started on his self-love in the pantry.) We also get a Scribe Virgin sighting; then she is dropped like a hot potato.<br /><br />The romance, itself, between Trez and Selena (before Ward killed her) was kind of meh. I had some issues with how she got so modern so fast. But my real complaint was in the melodrama. It didn't ring true. Maybe that's another reason why my emotions weren't engaged.<br /><br />The most interesting parts for me were in the few cut-scenes with Qhuinn's brother, Luchas. He is a messed up guy and with good reason. --And in the b-plot of Xcor and Layla. I feel something there. I liked where it was going, until he stomped all over it with a hooker.<br /><br />In the end of it all, I was just left tired... and disappointed. This is not what I signed up for as I committed myself to these 576 pages. After wading through all of the predictable, trite, and even downright ridiculous parts of the book, I should have had something to show for it. A happy freaking ending. Instead, I got a big, fat fail.<br /><br />If you want total spoilers from beginning to end: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://twitter.com/tweetasiread">http://twitter.com/tweetasiread</a><br /><br /><i>*ARC provided by publisher</i></span>

          </span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer985913452" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer17716344509796483440"><b>5 There is a thin line between love and hate Stars</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s327.photobucket.com/user/jessica_hatfield1/media/tumblr_nb5altFOXb1qikmd9o1_500_zps7vt6iok3.gif.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>

</a><br/><br/><b> There will be spoilers all over this bitch. Just saying!</b><br/><br/>First read 2015<br/>Reread April 16 2017 <br/><br/><b>Sometimes, the evil you fought wasn’t anything you could hit or shoot or dismember. Sometimes you couldn’t even hurt it. And that was really fucking awful.</b><br/><br/>There truly is a very thin line between love and hate and this book tap danced all over the borderline. I took hours after finishing this book trying to decide what to rate this book. What do I rate</span>
  <span id="freeText17716344509796483440" style="display:none"><b>5 There is a thin line between love and hate Stars</b><br><br><a href="http://s327.photobucket.com/user/jessica_hatfield1/media/tumblr_nb5altFOXb1qikmd9o1_500_zps7vt6iok3.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1443488188ra/16366259.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_nb5altFOXb1qikmd9o1_500_zps7vt6iok3.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b> There will be spoilers all over this bitch. Just saying!</b><br><br>First read 2015<br>Reread April 16 2017 <br><br><b>Sometimes, the evil you fought wasn’t anything you could hit or shoot or dismember. Sometimes you couldn’t even hurt it. And that was really fucking awful.</b><br><br>There truly is a very thin line between love and hate and this book tap danced all over the borderline. I took hours after finishing this book trying to decide what to rate this book. What do I rate a book that I both love and hate? One that made me laugh, smile, cry, scream and broke my heart all in one go. A book that kept me on edge even after I already read enough spoilers to know what was coming and still couldn't put it down. I rate that a 5 star read!<br><br><b>"Abruptly, Trez stopped breathing as he put the math together and came up with the impossible. Holy shit, that was the— “Hello, Mother,” Vishous said dryly. —Scribe Virgin. “I have come for a purpose.” The female voice was hard as crystal and just as clear. “And it must be served.” “Really.” V took a drag on his hand rolled. “You gonna take candy from a baby? Or is it kick a puppy night?”"</b><br><br><a href="http://s327.photobucket.com/user/jessica_hatfield1/media/5js9acjpg_zpsa4dbv17s.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1443488188ra/16366260.gif" alt=" photo 5js9acjpg_zpsa4dbv17s.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>“Courage doesn’t mean you aren’t scared.” He dropped his mouth to hers and kissed her. “God, I love you so much. I love you so deeply. I love you forever.”-Trez</b><br><br>I can't say I am shocked that J.R. Ward killed off Selena even before I read all the spoilers. I mean she killed off Darius and a pregnant Wellsie. Zsadist is a former blood slave that was raped, beat and imprisoned for years, Bella got kidnapped, beat, and tortured, John Matthew got raped, and Xhex got kidnapped and raped repeatedly by Lash. So no I am not surprised that J. R. Ward went dark. I would have been shocked if she didn't do something dark. That being said If you are looking for rainbows, flowers and everyone gets a HEA don't read this book. There is no HEA for Trez and Selena. There is a HEA for Iam and Maichen.<br><br><b>“You’re going to find someone else,” she moaned. “You’re going to fall in love with someone else and she’s going to be able to give you young and hold you when you have daymares and make you dinner.” The tears came so hard and heavy, she couldn’t take a breath. “And she’s going to be better than me because she’s going to…” Selena collapsed against him. “…she’s going to be lucky enough to be alive.”-Selena</b><br><br><a href="http://s327.photobucket.com/user/jessica_hatfield1/media/The%20shadows_zpsqpvawyen.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1492359150i/22508993._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo The shadows_zpsqpvawyen.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>“In all the time they’d known the guy, iAm had never paid any particular attention to the females. Or the males. Personally, Rhage had always thought the poor bastard was suffering from Phury Syndrome a condition whereupon one brother was so fucked-up that the other fell into a black hole trying to save him.” </b><br><br>As anyone who reads the BDB knows there are lots of side stories going on in each book, almost like a on going soap opera. Xcor and Layla's story is one I have been dying for since The King. When I first read of Xcor I hated him, then I soften to him, and then I loved him. So I was so looking forward to the bits and pieces I would get in this book about Layla and Xcor and for the most part I loved what I got. Till the end when Xcor pulled a douche move that made me wanna stomp his nuts. I mean Really Xcor? You are going to decide you can't be with Lalya and fuck a hooker? WTF??????????????<br><br><b>She is . . . the moon in my night sky. And that is the beginning, middle, and end of it. There is no more to be told than that, and never shall I speak of her again."-Xcor about Lalya</b><br><br><a href="http://s327.photobucket.com/user/jessica_hatfield1/media/stomp_em_in_the_nuts_by_5n0w-d4j2ybf_zpsvysgvwhs.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1443488188ra/16366262.gif" alt=" photo stomp_em_in_the_nuts_by_5n0w-d4j2ybf_zpsvysgvwhs.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>Then Manny said, “There is nothing I won’t do to keep her with him. Nothing.” Now Rhage was the one pulling the pivot. “That’s what I needed to hear, Doc.” “Just don’t put your faith in miracles, Hollywood. That’s a dangerous bet.” “It happened for me and Mary. When we needed one, we got one.” Manny stared out the front windshield—and didn’t appear to see anything of the darkened street ahead. “I’m not God. And neither is Doc Jane.”</b><br><br>Now because Xcor and Layla are not really together but have just been talking I don't really count it as cheating but I still don't like when heroes are with o/w regardless. So Xcor is going to have to really work hard to redeem himself in his book, whenever it comes out. (Soon Please J.R. Ward Please!!!) I enjoyed getting to know Paradise and meeting Craeg in this book. They are going to get their own book in a spin off series. <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/24903031.Blood_Kiss__Black_Dagger_Legacy___1_" title="Blood Kiss (Black Dagger Legacy, #1) by J.R. Ward" rel="nofollow noopener">Blood Kiss</a> I already like them. Especially Paradise who has a sassy side and is wanting to break out of the traditional roles of women and be more than a breeder. Woot girl power!<br><br><b>“Fuck you. I’m more than just a pair of ovaries you can put a ring on.”-Paradise</b><br><br><a href="http://s327.photobucket.com/user/jessica_hatfield1/media/giphy_zpsmhnwkzoq.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1443488188ra/16366263.gif" alt=" photo giphy_zpsmhnwkzoq.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>“Hey! Dragon boy Project Runway’s on if you wanna come watch. Maybe pick up some pointers on your threads.” Rhage’s stare narrowed, but he refused to look at the angel. “Isn’t there a Saved by the Bell marathon you have to go watch?” “Don’t hate on Zack. He’s like your little fucking brother, beauty queen.” -Lassiter </b><br><br>Assail I don't really care about. Loved getting to see Mary and Rhage again. It really pulled on my heartstrings that Rhage was having such a hard time with Trez and Selena and how it reminded him of almost losing Mary. I know <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/25293695.The_Beast__Black_Dagger_Brotherhood___14_" title="The Beast (Black Dagger Brotherhood, #14) by J.R. Ward" rel="nofollow noopener">The Beast</a> is coming out and I can't wait to get more of yummy Rhage. I will tell you who I really want to see more of, beside Xcor and Lalya of course because they are on top of my list and that is Qhuinn's brother Luchas. I need to see him get a HEA badly. OMG I want some more Luchas!! My poor Qhuinn. I think J.R. Ward is a extremely talented writer and I love The BDB series. This book wrung my heart out. My heart broke for Trez and Selena, but I seen a sad beauty to the time they had together. I hate that she dies and that Trez is left mourning, but like with <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/3473.A_Walk_to_Remember" title="A Walk to Remember by Nicholas Sparks" rel="nofollow noopener">A Walk to Remember</a> and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/15931.The_Notebook__The_Notebook___1_" title="The Notebook (The Notebook, #1) by Nicholas Sparks" rel="nofollow noopener">The Notebook</a> there is a sweetness to their love story. I think I will always be a huge J.R. Ward fan and I can't wait til the next book in this series. Below I leave a few quotes that moved me the most.<br><br><b>“Hey, on the outside chance the Grim Reaper is listening, I think he needs to know how much we hate his ass. Come on, my queen, say it with me. ‘Fuck you, death.’” She put her free hand up to hide an off-kilter smile. “You’re crazy.” “Tell me something I don’t know—and stop ducking this. ‘Fuck you, death!’” When she just mumbled the words, he shook his head. “Nope. Louder. ‘Fuck you, death!’” Selena started to laugh. “This isn’t funny.” “Couldn’t agree more.” He smiled and nodded at her, still poised with the ring at the top of her finger. “All together—like he can hear you.” “Fuck you, death!” she hollered. Then she smiled broadly. “Fuck you, death!”<br><br><br><br>“Do you think I’m happy about saying these things, thinking these things! I have God only knows how many nights left and I’ve wasted this one sitting on that fucking chair right there staring at some bullshit book I haven’t been reading, imagining you hanging yourself in a bathroom after I die! Or getting drunk and running your car into a tree! Or going on another fucking spree that lasts not a decade but a century!” She circled a finger next to her head. “These thoughts—I don’t want them! You think I want to tell you this? Jesus Christ, Trez, I love you! I don’t want you to ever be with another female, like ever! I want you to sit in a corner and mourn me until you die—I don’t want you to see the sun or the moon, or enjoy another meal, or have a good day’s sleep! I want to haunt you for the rest of your life, until everywhere you go and anyone you talk to, all you can see is the ghost of me—because then I know you won’t forget me!”<br><br><br><br>“This is real,” he told her. “You can trust this. You aren’t going to wake up and have this be over. You and I? This is our beginning.” “I love you,” she said in a rough voice. “I want no one else but you.” iAm smiled and pushed in between her legs, bringing his body against hers. “And I feel the same way, my maichen. I love you, I love you … I love you…”</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="17716344509796483440" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kellie Maddox-Ward" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kellie Maddox-Ward" href="/user/show/7309666-kellie-maddox-ward">Kellie Maddox-Ward</a>

          marked it as to-read

              <span id="reviewTextContainer902309033" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer4022675906856414545">I wonder what the new cover is going to look like? When the others have all been this hot? <br/><a href='http://s1150.photobucket.com/user/lil_kel4/media/blog%20cover%20reveals/output_gACtXv_zps3d3a9836.gif.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>

</a><br/><br/><b> SPOILERS SPOILERS SPOILERS! <br/>I’M NOT FUCKING AROUND THIS WAS TAKEN FROM THE CINCINNATI Q & A TRANSCRIPT APRIL 5TH 2014<br/>DO NOT READ UNLESS YOU <u>REALLY</u> WANT TO KNOW WHAT ELSE IS IN STORE FOR THE BDB! </b><br/>Personally I couldn’t wait and NEEDED to know what was coming. So if you are like me, read on! <br/>But If you don’t want to know. Seriously don’t read it! <br/><br/><a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[<br/><br/>Q: So what’s the next book?<br/>A: The Shadows….</span></span>
  <span id="freeText4022675906856414545" style="display:none">I wonder what the new cover is going to look like? When the others have all been this hot? <br><a href="http://s1150.photobucket.com/user/lil_kel4/media/blog%20cover%20reveals/output_gACtXv_zps3d3a9836.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1396762508ra/9184385.gif" alt=" photo output_gACtXv_zps3d3a9836.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b> SPOILERS SPOILERS SPOILERS! <br>I’M NOT FUCKING AROUND THIS WAS TAKEN FROM THE CINCINNATI Q &amp; A TRANSCRIPT APRIL 5TH 2014<br>DO NOT READ UNLESS YOU <u>REALLY</u> WANT TO KNOW WHAT ELSE IS IN STORE FOR THE BDB! </b><br>Personally I couldn’t wait and NEEDED to know what was coming. So if you are like me, read on! <br>But If you don’t want to know. Seriously don’t read it! <br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<br><br>Q: So what’s the next book?<br>A: The Shadows….and its about Trez and iAm…but, even better, guess who’s coming home???? MURHDER!!!!<br><br>Q: What’s going on with Selena?? What’s wrong with her joints???<br>A: She has a disease of the Chosen.<br>Q: Can they fix it?? What’s the disease???<br>A: Why would you read the book if I told you about it? (It’s genetic, but you’ll find out more in the book!<br><br>Q: The Queen of the Shadows is pregnant. Who’s the father:<br>A: The father is S’ex<br><br>Q: Are Rhage and Mary going to have a baby?<br>A: I know the answer but…Keep reading!!! Can’t say but wouldn’t surprise me if it came soon!<br><br>Q: What’s going on with the Scribe Virgin?<br>A: She needs some to re-engage her. It would be a surprise if she just came back to only to date Des…(laughter..nudge, nudge Desmond Hall…)<br><br>Q: Will JM ever know he’s Darius.<br>A: No, it would de-stabilize the world. I get asked that a lot. But I don’t think so…<br><br>Q: I think I’m the only one that cares, but…are you going to write a novella about the sympaths in that little camp?<br>A: Oh, no the sympaths are going to be trouble in the future.<br><br>Q: When’s my boy (John Matthew) going to become a Brother?<br>A: The timeline is a funny thing…it’s hard to show things that happen at the same time. The timelines get wonky sometimes. Tohr’s book was an entire year. Some books only take lkike..ten days. I think there needs to be something extraordinary that happens to get more Brothers in…that’s what she said…<br><br>Q: Also…prequels for all Brothers (AND FRITZ!!!)<br>A: That might be a good idea!<br><br>Q: Is Boo bonded to iAm???<br>A: (and JR does a selfie of the crowd before answering…) Absolutely. One of my favorite lines in the books was, “Goddamn cat”. And Fritz saying, we don’t have seafood in this house. And I know where you’re going with this…no, iAm is NOT banging the cat…geez…The reason the next book is called The Shadows is because iAm gets his too. iAm gets banged. (Lots of inappropriate comments related to cats…er…edited for good taste lol)<br><br>Q: Is the Lassiter part of the FA world.<br>A: Lassister was awesome was he not? He’s firmly in the BDB world. <br><br>Q: Last year you said boo was not exactly a cat. What is he exactly.<br>A: You’ll find out…maybe<br><br>Q: Is Immortal the last FA book.<br>A: Yes. There is something after but what we might find is how the FA and BDB intersect.<br><br>Q: When you were here last year, you told us a little secret about Tohr and Xcor…<br>A: I did? What did I say? (That they’re brothers…) I did??? I forgot that…. (laughter from crowd at JR’s forgetting she’d spilled those beans…) That will be coming out soon. The way Xcor and Layla’s situation is maturing, that’ll come to a head (Q: What is it?) I know,, but I’m not telling. But yes, Muhrder is coming back in the next book.<br><br>Q: Is Michael from The Story of Son going to come into the BDB world?<br>A: I could see how but it wouldn’t be any time soon.<br><br>Q: What about Saxton? Does he have an HEA?<br>A: Yes, you’ve met him. And no, it’s not iAm. iAm ends up with a chick, and Saxton ends up with a guy. <br><br>Q: Does Lash come back. <br>A: Yes…and he gets a girlfriend…and it’s Devina. (room goes crazy)<br><br>Q: Will you go back and do snippets for each Brother.<br>A: I was just talking to my editor about wanting to do more slices of life. The series needs to move or it dies. But it is something I’d like to do, to show small pieces of the Brothers’ lives. <br><br>Q: Will we see more of Qhuinn’s brother Lucas? What’s the deal with him. <br>A: We will see more of him. Yes, he will get better, but he has a long road. <br><br>Q: She wanted to know, if Wrath were to die, would Butch be the next in line?<br>A: Yes, Butch would be the next in line under the old ways. But that’s not the way we do it anymore.<br><br>Q: Why did they notify V about Payne’s fighting Wrath, rather than Manny?<br>A: I would say it’s like someone from a foreign country. Manny is not from this context, so, it was V who would take it harder and take it personally, as an insult. <br><br>Q: Where are the Hos…er…Chosen????<br>A: The Chosen are fluctuating between the Great Camp and the Sanctuary. (Why??) Because they can.(laughter) There are number of areas that are floating out there: The Chosen are one, the future of the training program is another. In the next few books, I’m hoping we’ll find out.<br><br>Q: What is Assail?<br>A: He is one hot motherfucker. (Hoots.) He’s a drug dealer. He’s a full-fledged vampire. <br><br>Q: Xcor and Throe, will there be a knockdown, drag out, fight between them?<br>A: When I met Throe, I thought he was such a good guy, but the more I get to know him…I think he has some bad juju. He’s beginning to make my skin crawl. At the end of the King, Xcor was softening. But Throe is ramping up.<br><br>Q: Is there a reason the Bloodletter doesn’t have a bloodline written?<br>A: It’s because they’re all such assholes…Well, okay, there’s always a reason for everything. The coffins in the garage, Boo…there’s always a reason, I just don’t know what it is. <br><br>Q: So, you have Qhuinn and Blay…will they do the traditional ceremony and get each other’s names on their backs. <br>A: Or Qhuinn has had Blay…but I think they will, its just not important to them.<br><br>Q: About JM…how will Wrath give him his scar, since he’s blind. <br>A: It will work out. JM will definitely have one.<br><br>Q: Will Lucas end up with Abalone’s daughter?<br>A: I don’t know. I know Abalone will hook up with someone, I just don’t know who. <br><br>Q: Have we met iAm’s woman?<br>A: You have not. <br><br>Q: Payne was so depleted at the end of Lover Unleashed.<br>A: She probably has to go to the Other side to replenish. She’s like a get-out-of-jail free card, but it wouldn’t surprise me that she eventually has to stop.<br><br>Q: Is anything going to happen to Havers, cause I wanted to chuck the hell out of him. <br>A: I wanted to throw my computer after that scene when he treated Layla like a vessel. One of the criticisms of the series is that its misogynistic, but I think it's changed and grown.<br><br>Q: My girl Xhex…will we see more of her?<br>A: I love her. Remember when she rejects JM, and he comes out of the bathroom stall? I love her and would to see more of her, and to see her fight. (How is she going to handle Murhder coming back.) She’s not but JM might skin him. <br><br>Q: Is Autumn Throe’s sister?<br>A: No, but his sister is the lynchpin around which two of your favorite characters spin.<br><br>Q: Will we see of Rehvenge and Ehlena?<br>A: I would love you to see more of Rehvenge and Ehlena. <br><br>Q: Is wrath 6’6” or 6”9”<br>A: He’s 6’9” and I’m dyslexic. (Laughter)<br><br>Q: Will there be a movie?<br>A: I write books not screen plays. If the right deal came along, I would consider it. But my job is to write the books. When you’re lucky like I am, you have to work and focus and do what makes you people like these books. I’m a writer, I’m not very interesting. So, I have to keep my focus on what keeps you liking the books. <br><br>Q: Are we going to hear from the glymera?<br>A: Yes, but they’ve really had their cock and balls cut, but they really have great ideas (eyerolls) and I’m looking forward to see what they are.<br><br>Q: Why didn’t we see that scene between Wrath and Tohr, at the pool house?<br>A: I know as a writer it’s my job to write but that scene was too personal which I know sounds weird, but I really think that sometimes there are things I can’t show…<br><br>Q: What’s the difference between the S’hibe(Sp?) the Moors, and the Shadows?<br>A: The S’hibe, the moors and the Shadows are all the same. Its different traditions referring to the same people. <br><br>Q: Will the fact that Xcor carved up the lesser have anything to do with Jose and Butch crossing paths again. <br>A: Jose and Butch will have closure. So, the one thing that hasn’t happened in the new world is that humans haven’t figured out that vampires exist. There’s a trajectory there that will tie it all together. <br><br>Q: Will Manny become a vampire?<br>A: Manny will never be turned. Payne can keep him young and perma-preserve him, and keep him alive. And the risk of turning is too high. <br><br>Q: Can you tell us about Lassiter? Will he fall in love?<br>A: He will fall in love. We will find out his purpose. It’s in the last scene in Immortal. <br><br>Q: I was like hoping that Lassiter would end up with the SV so V had to call him “Daddy”<br>A: (Laughter) That would almost be worth it. <br><br>Q: Is Wrath’s eyes from inbreeding or because of the poison when his mother was pregnant?<br>A: I don’t have an answer. The inbreeding makes sense. But I can’t say for sure. When I saw his mother get poisoned, that made sense, too, and I wondered. But Little Wrath doesn’t have that. It’s ironic that Beth being half-breed is what threatened his throne, but is what strengthened the gene pool. (Can Payne heal him) I’ve never seen Payne anywhere near his eyes, so I don’t think so.<br><br>Q: Are you going to tie in the Lessers and the FA series?<br>A: The Creator in the FA series is the Father of the SV and the Omega.<br><br>Q: What happens if the mansion gets raided?<br>A: The mhis covers the mountain but isn’t as thick at the bottom, and that’s one of the questions I’ve had. And, I think that’s where we’re going. <br><br>Q: How did you come up with the barbs on the male sympaths?<br>A: I didn’t think that shit up! That’s just what happened. That’s what he has in his pants! (Were you drunk?) I don’t drink…aren’t you glad? Maybe medication would be a good idea. (Laughter)<br><br>Q: Will see more of the O’Banyon brothers?<br>A: I would love to, but it’s whether I can carve out time for those.<br><br>Q: I loved the scene when Wrath’s mother comes to him in the dream. Will he ever get a glimpse of Little Wrath?<br>A: That was one of my favorite scenes. It was really cool, but really weird. I thought it was so great when he saw his mother. I was wondering if he was going to be preoccupied by whether his offspring would have the eye problems, but that wasn’t the issue at all. I think it would be wonderful for him to see Little Wrath, but I thought there would be an emotional issue if Little Wrath had his eyesight. And he was okay with it, he was all, I’m fine, so I don’t think it’s that important to him. <br><br>Q: Does Lassiter end up with a male or a female? And if it’s a male is it Saxton. <br>A: No, Lassiter likes girls. <br><br>Q:Assail is selling drugs to the enemy and contributing to the lessers. Does that make him the BDB enemy?<br>A: It’s a difficult situation. He sees it as using the Lessening society for his own purposes. But if shit goes down, he’s screwed. <br><br>Q: Can Xcor get his face fixed?<br>A: He absolutely can. He feels like, I’m ugly, and I don’t give a fuck. So I don’t know that it’s his priority.<br><br>Q: Do the BDB &amp; FA intersect?<br>A: Yes! The Creator in the FA series the Father of the SV and the Omega.<br><br>Q: What about the twins?<br>A: I love the twins. I went somewhere very bad. I LOVED Sola’s grandmother. Are you familiar with ghost peppers? Have you seen those Youtube videos about assholes who thinks it’s a great idea to eat them? And their faces go red? One of my favorite scenes is when the twins start eating these things and they have no reaction. And that’s Vovo’s first clue that there’s something weird there. Yeah, I think they’ll have HEAs…but NO! Not the same one!<br><br>Q: How far do you see the series extending?<br>A: The series is open-ended so as long as you want to read and the Brothers’ speak to me, I’ll keep writing!<br><br>Q: Will we ever find out the relationship between Rehvenge and the Shadows.<br>A: Yes, absolutely. <br><br>Q: Will Lassiter save Eddie. <br>A: No! (Does Eddies saved?) You’re going to have to read the book!<br><br>Q: Has Layla had her baby yet?<br>A: You’ll have to read the next book!<br><br>Q: I love that you wrote a respected, kick ass character who is blind, since my twin and I are blind. And I just wanted to tell you how much I loved the scene where Wrath tells the foremen that “I’m blind and it’s okay.” <br>A: I love that scene. It was one of my favorites for two reasons: so few people knew he was blind. That’s why the cover, without his shades, was so significant. <br> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_1243967133" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1243967133" />
    <a title="Tekla ✨" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3587456-tekla"><img alt="Tekla ✨" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1594926257p2/3587456.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1243967133?book_show_action=true">Apr 02, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Tekla ✨" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Tekla ✨" href="/user/show/3587456-tekla">Tekla ✨</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">not even my worst enemy</span></div>

        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1243967133" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7321815801612305676">I stopped reading this train-wreck after Qhuay's unsatisfying HEA. But I heard about the drama with JRW's newest BDB book and decided to take a look. To my surprise, among all the angry/disappointed and some still bizarrely positive reviews, there was <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/author_blog_posts/8124484-the-shadows-spoilers-spoilers' rel='nofollow noopener'>a post from her</a>. She knew she had fucked up so badly, she literally made a post to justify her book on the release day.<br/><br/>Let that sink in.<br/><br/>Now, this is not a review of The Shadows, since I haven't and won't read it, but a comment about her post and se</span>
  <span id="freeText7321815801612305676" style="display:none">I stopped reading this train-wreck after Qhuay's unsatisfying HEA. But I heard about the drama with JRW's newest BDB book and decided to take a look. To my surprise, among all the angry/disappointed and some still bizarrely positive reviews, there was <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author_blog_posts/8124484-the-shadows-spoilers-spoilers" rel="nofollow noopener">a post from her</a>. She knew she had fucked up so badly, she literally made a post to justify her book on the release day.<br><br>Let that sink in.<br><br>Now, this is not a review of The Shadows, since I haven't and won't read it, but a comment about her post and series in general. Why? Because I can and because what I read truly horrified me as a reader and former JRW fan. <br><br>These are some of the lines that stuck out the most to me, and a clear example of why everyone should avoid her books.<br><br><b>
  <i>"the idea of doing another Chosen falling in love (...) was a total snooze to me."</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1428000568ra/14349558.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>So... She's bored of her own storylines…? Okay.<br><br><br><b>
  <i>"I assumed that iAm would find his love, and Trez would find his cure for his female, and then yeaaaaaaaaaaaaaah, classic HEA sh*t all over the place!!!! Yawn. NOT THAT I DON'T LIKE MY HEAs. It's just that felt so predictable."</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1428000568ra/14349559.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>You mean predictable like all your other HEAs? Boring? Yawn inducting? Yeah, I couldn't agree more.<br><br><br><b>
  <i>"One of the issues with the Chosen is that (...) there isn't a lot of personality to them. "</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1393867274ra/8774745.gif" width="300" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Whose fault do you think it is that these characters have no personality and are boring to write <i>or read</i> about? I'm sorry, what did you say? Oh yeah, the author’s fault. <i>Shocking.</i><br><br><br><b>
  <i>"I suck at writing women"</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1384810993ra/6981983.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>She doesn't even bother to try and hide this anymore, I’m literally ???????? <br><br>Not only is JRW racist and sexist, <i>she's a bad writer.</i> She lives off her writing and she can't write female characters? After <i>12 books</i> writing M/F romance, she <i>still</i> can't write women?? It sounds like she didn’t even try, like she doesn't see where's the matter in saying she sucks at writing women, which says more than enough in itself. It just baffles me and honestly, I don't want to read a female author who has no idea how to write women. What does that say about her? Nothing good, that's what. <br><br>No wonder her gay men didn't use lube to have anal sex and one adopted "the girl" role in their relationship since JRW couldn't think outside of her heteronormativity box even if it hit her in the face. And don't get me started on her description of (the few) POC characters in her books. She literally compared someone to A TABLE. ("His skin was the color of the mansion’s mahogany dining room table") A fucking inanimate object. That's dehumanizing and offensive in so many ways, I don't understand how no one from her team of ass kissers didn't– oh right.<br><br>Not only does JRW have no idea how to write female characters, she's created one of the most sexist universes I've ever read. Women are owned by their husbands and treated like possessions and the males who are <i>decent human beings</i> to their women are considered swooning worthy because they could be total dicks to their wives but chose not to??????????? <br><br>The only female character who ever questions this is constantly described as manly and butch. Not just that, but she’s just like any other male character, only with (small) tits. Because for JRW, female characters don’t have any kind of personality unless it resembles a man’s. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1428004207ra/14350102.gif" width="300" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Let's remember Cormia being grateful because "Butch is old fashioned but he never complained about me working." <br><br>Let’s remember male characters asking other male characters to allow their women to do what they wanted to, because apparently women can’t decide on their own. <br><br>Let's remember the brothers literally being called an “anachronistic group of misogynists” in Lover Reborn. <br><br>Let’s remember the only gay couple having a female third wheel added permanently to their HEA because JRW wanted them to be daddies~ and apparently the only way to form a family is if you have children with someone from the opposite sex. <br><br>And let’s remember the “needing” and “servicing” bullcrap. JRW created an universe where women are unable to control their bodies or make decisions on their own and that’s supposed to be <i>romantic</i>. Lovely, isn't it? I've always wanted some dub-con in my life.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1428004460ra/14350126.gif" width="300" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>JRW's straight white cis privileges show in her writing as she insists on appropriating POC’s culture to write her white characters but hey, like JRW apparently said to the accusations of racism, that's not racist because they are not human, they are vampires!!!!!!! <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1393968368ra/8789044.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br>((SPOILERS FOR THE SHADOWS)) <br><br><br><br><br>How dumb can you be to write a paranormal romance and kill the main female character?????????????? My friend told me JRW did it to be controversial and have an edge. Well, I hope the edge hits her little toe someday. If you use your writing as a cathartic exercise to cleanse your soul and that's the reason why you kill your HEA in a romance novel, THEN YOU QUITE LITERALLY LEFT ALL YOUR SHIT ON YOUR READERS.<br><br>&lt; sarcasm &gt; ...... But ohhhh myyyy god, you don't understand, the man-pain made Trez so much more interesting!!!!!!! Thanks to Whatevers-her-name dying, his character could develop so much!!!!!!!!! Angst makes male characters so much better!!!!!!! And that's not sexist at all!!!!!!!!! &lt; / sarcasm &gt;<br><br><b>Edit:</b> I just found out Layla is in this book. I see reviews complaining about her obsession with getting laid while one of her sisters is dying. And because she kept lying to Qhuinn. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1399167300ra/9517492.gif" width="350" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>It sounds in character for Layla, though. ¯\_(ツ)_/¯ Apparently she also helps Qhuinn when he's having issues with his brother?? Of-fucking-course. After all, Qhuinn/Layla was the boring, predictable HEA she had planned from the start. <br><br>You know you've fucked up when <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/259807054?type=review#rating_33875301" rel="nofollow noopener">my 2 stars review of Lover Reborn</a> and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/305722885?type=review#rating_41102367" rel="nofollow noopener">my 1 star review of Lover At Last</a> started to get likes again in the last few days.<br><br>Lastly, whoever’s still reading her books: Please love yourself more. ♥<br><br></span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/905025759?book_show_action=true">Apr 08, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lucy Qhuay" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lucy Qhuay" href="/user/show/7115693-lucy-qhuay">Lucy Qhuay</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer905025759" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4476850834366571487"><br/>This is, without a doubt, one of the saddest books I've ever read and the saddest in the series so far. <br/><br/>Deep aching sorrow was my constant companion while reading and it's with me still. <br/><br/>Thinking about what happened, of course I wish for a different outcome.<br/><br/>However, and even though I understand some fans were left deeply angered with the way things turned out to be, I can't help but appreciate the beauty in the pain and harbour a small flicker of hope inside of me.<br/><br/>J.R.Ward is a talented writer. </span>
  <span id="freeText4476850834366571487" style="display:none"><br>This is, without a doubt, one of the saddest books I've ever read and the saddest in the series so far. <br><br>Deep aching sorrow was my constant companion while reading and it's with me still. <br><br>Thinking about what happened, of course I wish for a different outcome.<br><br>However, and even though I understand some fans were left deeply angered with the way things turned out to be, I can't help but appreciate the beauty in the pain and harbour a small flicker of hope inside of me.<br><br>J.R.Ward is a talented writer. There is no denying that after this book, since only a talented writer is able to give you something you hardly wanted, inflict great pain, leaving you completely emotionally drained, yet making it so that you can look deep into the abyss and appreciate the fall. <br><br>Trez and Selena's journey was that for me. It was like walking through a hidden path in some forgotten forest, looking around and contemplate thousands upon thousands of the most magnificent roses, as far as the eye can see. <br><br>Heart-shattering, magical even, but the road is narrow and full of thorns.<br><br>It was worth it, though. <br><br>I'll never forget them or the love they shared. I'll never forget how they lived a thousand lives in mere days. I'll never forget that they were meant to be and what they meant to each other.<br><br>And I sincerely hope that, if ever I am in the same position, I don't lose my way like they didn't.<br><br>I won't forget all the other characters and their struggles either. There was a lot to take in in this instalment and things weren't easy for anyone.<br><br>Trez. Selena. iAm. The Brothers. The shellans. s'Ex. maichen. They all suffered in some way and it was hard as hell to witness that, but I stand by my words that everything was worth it.<br><br>But the story goes on and I know J.R.Ward has a lot to give us still. This won't be the end.<br><br>I know there is something waiting along the way for Trez and that we'll see him in a different light. I can feel it.<br><br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<br><b> ---2014--- </b><br><br>Another book in this awesome series<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/480191.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>J. R. Ward...<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1397006292ra/9217611.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>And we have a freaking title<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1391541319ra/8408209.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>So. Damn. Hyped. For. This.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/580691.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Oh, yes! NEED...NEED...NEED<br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1397006292ra/9217612.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>I am so ready for this<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1397006292ra/9217613.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>And all kinds of this<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1397006292ra/9217614.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>I am not even ashamed of it<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1397006292ra/9217615.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>What I have to say to the haters<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1397006292ra/9217616.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
