  <span id="freeText13947762106686712795" style="display:none"><b>OMG. OMG. OMG. OMG.<br><br>The Shadows finally get a book! YAAAY<br><br>Hold Up!! Wait a minute!! <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ So there is no HEA for Trez?  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>BOOOOOO!!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1441353699ra/16098425.gif" width="400" height="234" alt="Dancing and Crying" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>****I Suffer from Mixed Emotions****<br><br>*****Not. Sure. How. To. Rate. This.****<br><br>Final review...with MEGA Spoilers ahead!!!<br>You have been Warned!!</b><br><br><br>J.R. Ward remains a brilliant writer, but I thought this series fell under the genre of paranormal romance? Apparently I was mistaken and this series has evolved into what ever the Warden wants it to be. Which means HEA's ( Happy Ever Afters) are no longer a guarantee. But excuse me...isn't that why I read romance novels??? So I can experience the ups and downs, all the drama and the angst, just to get to an ooey gooey ending that is full of Love and Feel Goods!!<br><br>Well, I am beyond torn on how to rate this hodgepodge experience. As always, The Warden introduces her readers to her next book, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/24903031.Blood_Kiss__Black_Dagger_Legacy___1_" title="Blood Kiss (Black Dagger Legacy, #1) by J.R. Ward" rel="nofollow noopener">Blood Kiss</a>, by starting the story in this one. We meet a very young vampire, Paradise. She's a sweet, strong minded girl and her story is basically a build up to her book, which will be released later this year. I can only hope it has a happy ending.<br><br><br>I loved the interaction of the brothers and the serious quality time with Rhage and his demons. <br><br><br><b>
  <i>"This is calm, cool, and collected, you little bitch. You don’t want to see me pissed off."</i>
</b><br><br><br>There were cameos from characters that I thought J.R. Ward had forgotten existed. Xhex, Payne, Autum, oh and the Scribe Virgin popped in briefly. They did't have speaking parts, but they were present. <br><br><br>Asail is still hanging around, even though his true love is down in Miami, living a crime free life without him. I'm still not sure why Asail keeps getting so much air time. Maybe he will be getting his own book someday down the road. But at this point, I could care less.<br><br><br>Layla and Xcor break my heart. Talk about falling in love with the absolute Wrong person! <br><br><br><b>
  <i>She is . . . the moon in my night sky. And that is the beginning, middle, and end of it. There is no more to be told than that, and never shall I speak of her again.</i>
</b><br><br><br>Gah, I used to look forward to these two to getting their own book. But ENOUGH ALREADY!!! Their so called affair/ forbidden romance has been dragging on for 3+ books already. I CAN'T TAKE IT ANYMORE!!!<br><br><br>Now to the main story of the Shadows. There were two love stories, Trez and Selena, and iAm and his secret lover. I wanted a happy ending for Trez, to counter balance his entire life of misery. <br><br><br><b>Trez</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1430236830i/14696512._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="308" alt="d" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>Trez blew out his breath. “You know what my fantasy is? It ain’t porn. It’s good news. For once in my fucking life, I’d love to have some good news."</i>
</b><br><br><br>Well, he sure as hell didn't get any good news in this book. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[The love of his life died in his arms.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><br><b>Selena</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1417798625i/12548427._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="542" alt="d" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Selena's character was a total joy and was one of my favorite heroines. She was honest, strong, and determined to live her life to the fullest. Her time with Trez was beautifully written and beyond bittersweet. Oh and did I mention the tear jerker roller coaster ride of emotions. The Warden is very talented that way. I'm talking Ugly crying!!! Have a box of klenex and a bottle of alcohol close by. <br><br><br>But I can not in anyway condone <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[allowing your heroine to not only die, but then be burned on a pyre!! <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> Everyone with access to books on healing, i.e. Manny, Doc Jane, Rehvenge, and even iAm, could find no cure for Selena. But no one asked Payne to work her voodoo healing magic. NOT ONE PERSON, not even the Primale, approached the Scribe Virgin and asked for help or offered a sacrifice for Selena. For her to have been so loved by everyone...nobody, not even the Chosen went to ask the mother of their race to save her. <b>What a Fucking Joke!!! I mean, WTH??</b><br><br>I used to LOVE the BDB series. I have gotten countless other readers addicted to the series by offering friends my paperback copies of books 1-3. But I now find myself telling them to stop reading after book 5 (Vishous and Jane). Phury's book was a Disaster. Tohr's book was a Hot Mess. Blay and Qhuinn got ripped off and shafted. They may have only had ⅓ of the space in their book. The rest was nonsense about other couples no one cared about.<br><br>This series is no longer an auto buy, and hasn't been since I purchased <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13570854.Lover_at_Last__Black_Dagger_Brotherhood___11_" title="Lover at Last (Black Dagger Brotherhood, #11) by J.R. Ward" rel="nofollow noopener">Lover at Last</a>. I just wait for my local library copy, because I am no longer impressed by J.R. Ward's "Rice Crispies", or her Paranormal Soap Opera of characters, or her Non Happy, Sad as Hell Endings!!</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="13947762106686712795" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/901907296?book_show_action=true">Apr 05, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lenore" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lenore" href="/user/show/5299266-lenore">Lenore</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer901907296" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4517884605973381555"><b>ETA on 11 April 2015: Please see at the bottom of my review.</b><br/><br/>1.5 stars rounded up.<br/><br/>First of all, I would like to clarify that the <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/author_blog_posts/8124484-the-shadows-spoilers-spoilers' rel='nofollow noopener'>blog</a> J.R. Ward posted on release day of The Shadows played a major role in my opinion and my rating of this book.<br/><br/>J.R. Ward attributes everything she puts on paper to her Rice Krispies, assuming the role of the Delphic Oracle, or that of a mere conduit who doesn't have a say in her own work. <br/><br/>She also keeps breaking her own rules, conveniently forgetting that writing fant</span>
  <span id="freeText4517884605973381555" style="display:none"><b>ETA on 11 April 2015: Please see at the bottom of my review.</b><br /><br />1.5 stars rounded up.<br /><br />First of all, I would like to clarify that the <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author_blog_posts/8124484-the-shadows-spoilers-spoilers" rel="nofollow noopener">blog</a> J.R. Ward posted on release day of The Shadows played a major role in my opinion and my rating of this book.<br /><br />J.R. Ward attributes everything she puts on paper to her Rice Krispies, assuming the role of the Delphic Oracle, or that of a mere conduit who doesn't have a say in her own work. <br /><br />She also keeps breaking her own rules, conveniently forgetting that writing fantasy (paranormal or otherwise) and creating your own world isn't a get-out-of-jail-free-card and it doesn't mean that anything goes. Especially not in a romance series, despite the urban fantasy elements. <br /><br />For instance: You can't have your deity (the Scribe Virgin) save one heroine (Mary) from certain death, curing her end-stage leukaemia, Deus-Ex-Machina-style, or bring another heroine (Jane) back from the dead as a ghost, or have yet another heroine (Autumn) survive her own suicide for centuries, then ascend to the Fade (J.R. Ward's version of heaven) Jesus-style and then bring her back because "oops, she can't die", and you can't have the deity's daughter (Payne) do her hocus pocus and reverse a spontaneous abortion, or have her act as a font of eternal youth who will keep her human husband (Many) and the king's seeing eye dog (George) alive for evermore, <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[AND THEN shrug and let another heroine die of a JOKE of a disease, putting her down and out of her misery like a dog because why not, meh, she was uninteresting anyway.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> It doesn't work like that. You can't play god and arbitrarily change the rules as you deem convenient. It's disrespectful to yourself, your work, and your audience.<br /><br />What follows is an imaginary discussion between J.R. Ward and her editor:<br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<br /><b>[J.R. Ward &amp; her editor on IM]</b><br /><br /><b>J.R. Ward:</b> I just emailed you my first draft. Fair warning: It's a sloppy mess. Oh also, I killed the heroine.<br /><b>Editor:</b> *gapes* Why??<br /><b>J.R. Ward:</b> Meh. She was uninteresting. And I suck at writing female characters anyway. So.<br /><b>Editor:</b> *still gaping* But… Wasn't there *any* other way?<br /><b>J.R. Ward:</b> Maybe. I don't know. I didn't know what to do with her so whatever. I killed her off. <br /><b>Editor:</b> *crickets*<br /><b>J.R. Ward:</b> Right. So hit me when you're done going over it. Dot my i's and cross my t's, editor extraordinaire! *thumbs up emoji* *toothy grin emoji*<br /><br /><b>[A few weeks later, over the phone]</b><br /><br /><b>Editor:</b> I just sent you my editorial letter with a couple of suggestions on macro edits.<br /><b>J.R. Ward:</b> Yeah, I'm opening the attachment as we speak.<br /><b>Editor:</b> It's a good story. I'm sure we can work something out.<br /><b>J.R. Ward:</b> WTF! This is three pages long!<br /><b>Editor:</b> Like I said, I just have *a couple of* suggestions.<br /><b>J.R. Ward:</b> This is too much!<br /><b>Editor:</b> Trust me. Three pages is really—<br /><b>J.R. Ward:</b> No way!<br /><b>Editor:</b> —not that much…<br /><b>J.R. Ward:</b> Did I mention that my dog died and I'm sad and I want that to be reflected in my work?<br /><b>Editor:</b> I'm really sorry. Maybe you could write something else, a standalone maybe or a short story, to express your sorrow?<br /><b>J.R. Ward:</b> I don't have time for this!<br /><b>Editor:</b> I understand, but this is not how this world usually works—<br /><b>J.R. Ward:</b> I've explained how my Rice Krispies work, editor!<br /><b>Editor:</b> But if you switched Trez &amp; Selena's story with iAm &amp; Catra's, making the latter the main plot and the former a minor subplot, it might work a bit better—<br /><b>J.R. Ward:</b> My Rice Krispies can't have this shit!<br /><b>Editor:</b> That's how the Wellsie thing happened and it was mostly okay…<br /><b>J.R. Ward:</b> Did you hear what I just said about my Rice Krispies? I don't have a say in this.<br /><b>Editor:</b> Please consider it? You're a professional. It might make more sense to—<br /><b>J.R. Ward:</b> YOU INSOLENT NOBODY! ARE YOU TELLING ME HOW TO WRITE MY BOOKS? Is that what you're doing?<br /><b>Editor:</b> No, of course not. I'm just trying to help—<br /><b>J.R. Ward:</b> *hangs up*<br /> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />I'm not rating low because of <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[the non-HEA <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. It could have worked if J.R. Ward had put some actual effort into it, if she had convinced me there was no other way, if it weren't so sloppy and ridiculous and, well, lazy writing for shock value and emotional impact over any sort of sense, consistency, or realism within the rules of the world she herself has created.<br /><br />With this book, J.R. Ward is mocking me as her reader: <i>Here, brainless fan who will gobble down anything I put out like a modern Pythia in trance. Read this.</i><br /><br />Well… I'll say this. I WILL be reading the future instalments because I'm interested in learning what happens next with a few of the plot lines, but I won't be rushing to pre-order them anymore. Not unless I learn what happens beforehand, and not unless J.R. Ward proves she can win back my trust as a loyal reader.<br /><br /><b> ETA:<br />For a detailed breakdown of all the things that haven't been working in the series in general, and in The Shadows specifically, see Beanbag's <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1243351991?book_show_action=false" rel="nofollow noopener">review</a> and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/story/show/396494?chapter=1" rel="nofollow noopener">blog post</a> here on Goodreads.</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="4517884605973381555" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1099288126?book_show_action=true">Nov 06, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Laura" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Laura" href="/user/show/8429172-laura">Laura</a>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1099288126" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2953142243713341847"><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1420429845ra/13223235.gif' width='500' height='245' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>|4.3 my feels are all over the floor stars|<br/><br/><i>You know, I think I need to lay down and think about what I just read...</i><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1428717420ra/14474271.gif' width='400' height='230' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I've been reading these series since 2006 (soon 10 fucking years, OMG!!!) and I always feel like being home. Want me to get all nostalgic? Make me read some J.R. Ward and that's it. I'll always going to have a soft spot for her and these series.<br/><br/>That being said I really <i>really</i> enjoyed this book. I mean, it was a very heavy reading and I was <b>way too</b> invested in the story, so for me it</span>
  <span id="freeText2953142243713341847" style="display:none"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1420429845ra/13223235.gif" width="500" height="245" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>|4.3 my feels are all over the floor stars|<br><br><i>You know, I think I need to lay down and think about what I just read...</i><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1428717420ra/14474271.gif" width="400" height="230" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I've been reading these series since 2006 (soon 10 fucking years, OMG!!!) and I always feel like being home. Want me to get all nostalgic? Make me read some J.R. Ward and that's it. I'll always going to have a soft spot for her and these series.<br><br>That being said I really <i>really</i> enjoyed this book. I mean, it was a very heavy reading and I was <b>way too</b> invested in the story, so for me it was actually quite difficult to read and finish.<br><br>And maybe I'm growing old but I wasn't <i>that</i> happy with the multiple POVs this time and I kinda missed the old days when there were only three or four POVs. It wasn't all bad because I loved <u>almost</u> all the characters.<br><br>Yep, you know who I didn't like? Assail.<br>Remember I used to like Assail? Well, I don't know what the heck was wrong with me at the time. He's an despicable man, a drug addict who does nothing good nor interesting. Now I know that I only <i>liked</i> him when Sola and her grandmother were involved. I'm pathetic, I know.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1428714554ra/14474015.gif" width="400" height="230" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>So, let's go to the MCs.<br><br>I've always liked iAm better than Trez. iAm was kinder and sweeter than Trez but, boy, didn't he win me over at the end. You gotta love a man who loves so much and so hard.<br><br>The whole situation with Selena was absolutely sad and I felt hopeless most of the time. I just couldn't see any way out.<br><br>I just, man, I still don't know. I usually take my time with these books because it's a lot to handle.<br><br>I don't know how things are going to work out for Layla and Xcor.<br>On that note, I really don't like all the hate Layla always gets. I mean, what's up with that? How could people hate on her? What has she done? And I mean before the thing with Xcor because she's getting all that hate way before that.<br>What? Because she fucked with Qhuinn? Oh, get over yourselves. She wanted and baby he wanted a baby and she was in her needing period. Done. Layla has been nothing but kindess and support without asking for anything. She was the <i>first Chosen</i> we knew and she was a window of oportunities. She was good with Rhage and Mary, she's been always there for <b>all</b> the Brothers so maybe I'm taking it a bit too personal but what the fuck?<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1428717287ra/14474242.gif" width="400" height="230" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Anyhow, Trez and Selena... they were really good together. I liked Selena enough and that ending. I swear, I almost lose my shit and Trez was so heartbroken, gods, awful.<br><br>This book was way too painful.<br><br>iAm and the maid were really cute. One of my favorite couples, I think. Although their relationship felt rushed at times, they got to know each other better and that was great to see. <br><br>iAm, lord...<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1428717287ra/14474243.gif" width="245" height="175" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And Rhage? JFC, I didn't know how much I missed him until I read his POV. I missed him a lot and I'm so fucking happy we're getting another book about him and Mary next year!!<br><br>I also liked Parry and Craeg. I'm looking forward to reading <i>Blood Kiss</i> this December.<br><br><b>I'm counting on Zsadist's book to be the next one after Rhage's because I need some of my <i>Hellren</i> and Bella and Nalla!</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="2953142243713341847" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_2561644025" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2561644025" />
    <a title="Ꮗ€♫◗☿ ❤️ ilikebooksbest.com ❤️" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/70316517-ilikebooksbest-com"><img alt="Ꮗ€♫◗☿ ❤️ ilikebooksbest.com ❤️" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1570843185p2/70316517.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2561644025?book_show_action=true">Nov 15, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ꮗ€♫◗☿ ❤️ ilikebooksbest.com ❤️" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ꮗ€♫◗☿ ❤️ ilikebooksbest.com ❤️" href="/user/show/70316517-ilikebooksbest-com">Ꮗ€♫◗☿ ❤️ ilikebooksbest.com ❤️</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/70316517-ilikebooksbest-com?shelf=vampires">vampires</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/70316517-ilikebooksbest-com?shelf=alphas">alphas</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/70316517-ilikebooksbest-com?shelf=urban-fantasy">urban-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/70316517-ilikebooksbest-com?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/70316517-ilikebooksbest-com?shelf=erotic-romance">erotic-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2561644025" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14432034814495488930"><b>The Shadows and the Brotherhood.</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1573973135i/28461863.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Truly a great book. The main romance in this book is that of Trez and the chosen Selena. Though one thing that I really like about these BDB books is that each of them don’t just focus on the main romance storyline, they have other storylines being set up, ongoing storylines that go from book to book, and so much going on in every single book. <br/><br/>It is a genius way too keep people interested and wanting to read more. Otherwise 20+ books (Black Dagger Brotherhood and </span>
  <span id="freeText14432034814495488930" style="display:none"><b>The Shadows and the Brotherhood.</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1573973135i/28461863.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Truly a great book. The main romance in this book is that of Trez and the chosen Selena. Though one thing that I really like about these BDB books is that each of them don’t just focus on the main romance storyline, they have other storylines being set up, ongoing storylines that go from book to book, and so much going on in every single book. <br><br>It is a genius way too keep people interested and wanting to read more. Otherwise 20+ books (Black Dagger Brotherhood and Black Dagger Legacy), that are 500-600 pages would get too be way too much after a while. I took about a 5 month break after 11 books and even now that I am back to them, I am thinking two at a time is plenty before I read something else for a few weeks or so. However, I know that I will go back to them for certain because I just have to know what happens in some of these ongoing storylines and if certain people will end up together.<br><br>The next book is The Beast and this book is setting that one up, because Rhage and Mary play a big role in this book. Rhage is having some odd attacks that may or may not be related to stress and anxiety. I love the story of Rhage and Mary because he is as hot as a blonde God, his nickname is Hollywood because of his movie star good looks, but he fell in love with an average looking woman. It is usually the other way around, where average looking guys end up with fabulous looking women (though they usually are average looking wealthy guys) so not the same thing at all. It is just nice to see.<br><br>An ongoing storyline in this book is the continuing saga of Assail, the drug dealer. I had high hopes for him and Sola in the last book, but she wanted to get away from a dangerous and illegal lifestyle, and as much as Assail loves her, it doesn’t seem to be enough to give up his drug dealing. And what is it sometimes with these rich men in books? How come being rich is never enough? They have to keep making more money even though we know they could never spend it all. Once you have millions or billions, the money just sits there making more by itself from investments and interest I would think.<br><br>Assail is getting in trouble with the Brotherhood in this book because they found out he is selling to the enemy. The lessers are using the money they make on the drugs they get from Assail, to buy automatic weapons for their war against the vampires. I don’t really get it since in the drug trade, I’m sure there are plenty of buyers that aren’t people who want to kill your race. It’s like selling bombs to terrorists, but people do it. I am hoping Assail sees the light and stops, because I still want him to end up with Sola. I loved the interaction between her Grams and Assail, Avale and Ehric.<br><br>The story of Xcor and Layla continues in this book also. Xcor and Layla meet often and he has blackmailed her into agreeing to be with him. Though Xcor won’t take her while she is pregnant since he is not gentle and doesn’t want to hurt the baby. Layla is riddled with guilt about meeting with him. Though she tells herself she is doing it for the King, the Brotherhood and the cause, we as readers know that she really wants him but doesn’t want to want him. <br><br>Layla also has a storyline with Qhuinn and Blaylock since Quinn is the father of her baby. That gets interesting as well, but I’m not going to give anything away as to why. I try to stick to only background information in my reviews so the reader and I (as I look back on my own reviews), can see what the book is about without giving away what actually happens. <br><br>Another storyline is the ongoing struggle between Quinn and his brother, Luchas. After the massacre of many of the Glymera, including Qhuinn’s parents, Luchas was taken by Lessers and shoved in a drum with the black sludge from the Omega, having had his bones all broken. Then the Lessers forgot about him with all the changes of the forelessers. He Brotherhood found him at some point and he has been in the clinic at the mansion since Doctors Jane and Manny have tried to fix him in a very lengthy and painful process. Luchas feels guilt for how he treated Qhuinn and wants to die. <br><br>I personally think Luchas wants to die for two reasons aside from his guilt. The first is because he is a wimp and doesn’t want to go through more pain (though his pain is terrible, I think any of the Brotherhood would go through it). Second because if he doesn’t completely heal he will think of himself as less, like he always thought of his brother because Qhuinn had two different colored eyes.<br><br>The main story centers around Trez and Selena. Trez is one of the Shadows. They are an offshoot of the vampires that have a lot of the same Vampire traits like strength, speed, ability to dematerialize etc. However, they are dark skinned, they can bend shadows to conceal themselves, they can go out in daylight, they eat their prey after a fight (cannibalistic), and the Brotherhood is happy to have them on their side, so they must be tougher than the vampires as well. <br><br>Trez and iAm come from the s’Hsibe which is a colony of their people near the colony of Sympath’s in the North, near the Canadian border. Nobody leaves the s’Hsibe, but Trez escaped and iAm followed years ago after their parents sold Trez to the Queen to be the mate of her daughter who will one day be queen. The reason the s’Hsibe didn’t just accept the loss and get another guy forth Princess is because they have strange customs regarding things written in the stars and apparently their astrologists looked at the stars and decided that Trez was the anointed one, so the s’Hsibe are coming for Trez soon.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1574159278ra/28475101.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>The S’Hsibe have other customs like the fact that Trez would be basically owned by the princess and would be basically a slave and not able to leave his gilded cage. Also they have strict mating customs, like having to be clean and they bathe before and after the act. If they knew about all of the women Trez had been with, they will either kill him or put him through some sort of cleansing that may or may not kill him. <br><br>Trez has fallen for Selena and in this book he finds out her secret and she finds out his. It is a very emotional book, but their romance is sweet in a way that is different than most. Everyone in the Brotherhood does whatever they can for them, including longtime friend Rehvenge and iAm. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1574159278i/28475102._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>There is a storyline about iAm in this book also, which I am glad about since in the past we have seen him always doing things for his brother, pretty much devoting his life to save Trez, not only from the s’Hsibe but from Trez himself and his self destructive behaviors. It was nice to find out more about iAm as a person rather than just an extension of Trez.<br><br>There is also a storyline related to the s’Hsibe Queen’s executioner. His name is s’Ex. He is built like a brick building with abs, and though he understands the two brothers, he is sworn to his duty, so he tells them he will kill in order to get Trez back when it comes time. Though he does take some bribes in order to help them stall for time. He is a very interesting character in his own right. He is covered from neck to feet in the white tattoos of their people, made from poison ink. Most males have a small one with their family insignia on themselves and get extremely sick after having it. Trez and iAm can’t imagine how strong he must be to be covered in them. I hope he gets a mating story at some point.<br><br>The ending of the book was awesome. I think this was one of the best so far. My other two favorites so far are Lover Awakend, the story of Zsadist and Bella and Lover at Last, the story of Qhuinn and Blaylock. I liked Zsadist’s story because he is so fearsome and angry but he protects Bella so awesomely, and Lover at last because it was the single hottest male/male love story I have ever read and I had been wanting Qhuinn and Blay to fix things between them for a long time. <br><br><a href="https://www.ilikebooksbest.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Blog</a>|<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/wennel" rel="nofollow noopener">Goodreads</a>|<a href="https://www.facebook.com/ilikebooksbest" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook</a>|<a href="https://smile.amazon.com/gp/profile/amzn1.account.AFFE5A2BGXJQTQMCYHFC4YHV6KFQ?preview=true" rel="nofollow noopener">Amazon</a>|<a href="https://www.twitter.com/wendysu020202" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a>|<a href="https://www.bookbub.com/profile/1895823057" rel="nofollow noopener">BookBub</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="14432034814495488930" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_1243351991" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1243351991" />
    <a title="Beanbag Love" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2598237-beanbag-love"><img alt="Beanbag Love" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1249531311p2/2598237.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1243351991?book_show_action=true">Apr 01, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Beanbag Love" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Beanbag Love" href="/user/show/2598237-beanbag-love">Beanbag Love</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1243351991" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5476736138663707188">Popular author: "Hey, come over here, I want to show you something!<br/>Popular author's fan: "OMG! Of course. I've been waiting a whole year for you to show me something! I'm so excited!"<br/>Popular author: "Here, look ..."<br/><br/><a href='http://photobucket.com/images/penguin%20gif' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1427936076ra/14339767.gif' alt='penguin gif photo: Penguin slap 70166023_l.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>And now for the full report. So long some of it had to be my first GR blog post.<br/><br/>I’m an addicted reader. If you see me, there is a Kindle or a book somewhere on my person. It’s how I spend most of my free time. I love reading all kinds of stories, but mostly I love Romance. I read </span>
  <span id="freeText5476736138663707188" style="display:none">Popular author: "Hey, come over here, I want to show you something!<br>Popular author's fan: "OMG! Of course. I've been waiting a whole year for you to show me something! I'm so excited!"<br>Popular author: "Here, look ..."<br><br><a href="http://photobucket.com/images/penguin%20gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1427936076ra/14339767.gif" alt="penguin gif photo: Penguin slap 70166023_l.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>And now for the full report. So long some of it had to be my first GR blog post.<br><br>I’m an addicted reader. If you see me, there is a Kindle or a book somewhere on my person. It’s how I spend most of my free time. I love reading all kinds of stories, but mostly I love Romance. I read <i>a lot </i>of different genres, but I always come back to Romance. And, being a voracious reader, I admire and appreciate the hell out of authors. Finishing a story is so difficult and putting themselves out there with their creative endeavors has got to be incredibly daunting.<br><br>But I admire Romance authors the most. Of all fiction genres, I think they have the hardest job. Romance authors have the incredibly difficult task of making the impossible possible. Writing a story that engages the emotions, challenges belief and then delivers a satisfying <i>”happily ever after”</i> for the appreciative and expectant reader. Many, many authors fail at achieving all the elements that make a romance great. Many fall back on tropes and clichés and big misunderstandings (both a trope <i>and</i> a cliché). Many contrive stupid obstacles that make no sense and then apply an unbelievable twist at the end to bring a couple together. But I admire them all anyway for taking on something so overwhelming; making the impossible possible. And when an author is at the top of their game, it can be absolutely sublime to slip between those pages with those characters and live their story with them. Trusting, of course, that the author will have your back in the end.<br><br>I tend to give Romance authors and their stories a lot more slack than I do other authors and genres. Because I know how hard their job is and I appreciate that even if nothing else works in the story I can trust in that one thing. That ending. It may not be high literature, but there’s no trusting high literature on that point as fabulous as the writing might be. Romance, though … <i>that</i> I can trust.<br><br>Which brings me to The Shadows. <br><br>Because trust is important to me, and Romance as a genre is also important to me, I rate it on a different scale than I do other genres. As I said, I give it a bit more slack. Without that trust, the scale changes. Hence the dreaded LIST O’ PROBLEMS some have seen in a few of my previous reviews of non-romance authors. I read a lot of Urban Fantasy. Some of it is Romantic Urban Fantasy (where you end up with one couple) and I love it. Sometimes, in Urban Fantasy, there is <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[death <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. But these authors <i>do the work</i> when <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[death occurs to one of their characters <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. That’s a <i>lot</i> of work, make no mistake. A lot of research and plotting before they get to <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[the sob-inducing death scene and its aftermath <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. JRW did not do that work here. Doesn’t seem to have even tried. And that’s a shame. Because the end result might have worked for me otherwise. <br><br>I know a lot of people loved The Shadows. I don’t begrudge them that. I know they’re sensitive about it and protective of JR Ward in the aftermath. I gotcha. As I said in the comments, I’m a diehard fan. I’m a mod in one of the GR fan groups. I was a member of every message board JRW had since soon after Lover Unbound. I follow her on Facebook. Yes, there’s disappointment in how this book ended, but there are many more problems than just that. I’ll address these problems first and then I’ll address the Big Issue.<br><br>I go in depth here:<br><br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.goodreads.com/story/show/396494?chapter=1">https://www.goodreads.com/story/show/...</a><br><br>Let me end by saying that I am still a die hard fan of JR Ward’s Black Dagger Brotherhood. I’m disappointed in the choices <i>she</i> made in The Shadows, but that’s not going to stop me reading the series for now. I almost left before over a possible adultery plot line but was brought back by a friend. And that’s why I stay. Because through this series I’ve made a number of lovely friends that I enjoy so much. The community of our fan group is wonderful and I adore sharing the BDB experience with them. So I’m still in. Sadly, I don’t trust though, and it will no longer have the same value to me it once had. It was a comfort zone and it was special, and now it can’t be that again. <br><br>So we’ll see what the future brings for the Black Dagger Brotherhood. It’s a new era and a new ratings scale, which is why this one only received two stars. I hope, on this new path to something other than Romance we’ll get more detail, action, plausibility and continuity, and less maudlin inner monologue and jarring world glitch. Fingers crossed on that score. I do have hope.<br><br>ETA: And now I'm freaking pissed. PISSED! Just two weeks after this expensive book releases and the price has dropped to under $7 for the Kindle version. Similar price drop for the HC. Way to kick fans in the teeth ... again. (I know JRW didn't set the prices, but this just adds to the major disappointment of this whole debacle)<br><br>ETA2: Why did my rating disappear? The review stayed up but the star rating was blank. Seems fishy. <a href="http://s268.photobucket.com/user/zkatsmilies/media/confused0077.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1428302297ra/14402568.gif" alt="oh rly photo confused0077.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="5476736138663707188" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_1247711963" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1247711963" />
    <a title="Laura" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2043222-laura"><img alt="Laura" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1577660807p2/2043222.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1247711963?book_show_action=true">Apr 06, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Laura" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Laura" href="/user/show/2043222-laura">Laura</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2043222-laura?shelf=d-n-f">d-n-f</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1247711963" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2342278753726540">Read this review on <a href='http://www.gotfiction.com/dnf-review-the-shadows-by-jr-ward/' rel='nofollow noopener'>Got Fiction? book blog</a><br/><br/>Original Review:<br/><br/>*heavy sigh*<br/><br/>No.<br/><br/>I have to get my thoughts together on this one, but no. No more. I'm done with this.<br/><br/>Full Review:<br/><br/><b>*********SPOILERS ALL AROUND*********</b><br/><br/>Wow. Where to begin. So I'm not sure how many of you are aware of the spoiler that JR Ward posted, but I'm grateful she did. I decided not to buy this book after reading it. But after a few days online and seeing the reactions, I figured I owed it to you guys to write an informed review of why</span>
  <span id="freeText2342278753726540" style="display:none">Read this review on <a href="http://www.gotfiction.com/dnf-review-the-shadows-by-jr-ward/" rel="nofollow noopener">Got Fiction? book blog</a><br /><br />Original Review:<br /><br />*heavy sigh*<br /><br />No.<br /><br />I have to get my thoughts together on this one, but no. No more. I'm done with this.<br /><br />Full Review:<br /><br /><b>*********SPOILERS ALL AROUND*********</b><br /><br />Wow. Where to begin. So I'm not sure how many of you are aware of the spoiler that JR Ward posted, but I'm grateful she did. I decided not to buy this book after reading it. But after a few days online and seeing the reactions, I figured I owed it to you guys to write an informed review of why I didn't want to read it. And perhaps it would have surprised me? I decided to put my money where my mouth is.<br /><br />Many many of my friends were torn on this book. Some whose taste is so similar to mine, loved it! Others, felt betrayed.<br /><br />I felt betrayed.<br /><br />But I knew this from reading A) reviews B) JR Ward’s spoiler. Words from the author’s own mouth are what decided this for me. I knew I wouldn’t like it, I knew how it would end...and yet...I still had hope.<br /><br />Ward's spoiler link <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author_blog_posts/8124484-the-shadows-spoilers-spoilers?page=1" rel="nofollow noopener">here</a><br /><br />For example, if I see cheating...I know it’s a hard line for me. I won’t like it. I know my taste. I know whose reviews I can trust to have similar issues. So when I see that heroine dies, but isn’t saved miraculously, I’m out. I'm supposed to read almost 600 pages and NOT get a happy ending? Are you serious? We joked on twitter comparing this to a Nicholas Sparks novel, but the reality is that with Sparks, you know what you’re getting into, he doesn't call his books romance, <b>AND HE DIDN’T SPEND 13 BOOKS SETTING UP HEAs IN A WORLD WE’VE COME TO LOVE.</b><br /><br />That is the worst part of all of this; I feel lied to. You don't spend years building up a Paranormal Romance series, and base, and fans galore, just to slap them in the face. <br /><br /><b>She broke my trust.</b><br /><br />As an author, I will tell you, part of the plotting of a Romance novel is that you try your hardest to find some insurmountable defining Black Moment, and you make your characters overcome it. They win, they endure, they survive the trials we authors throw at them. They don't get an easy happy ending, they have to earn it.<br /><br />As a reader, you pick up a romance novel knowing that you have a hero and a heroine who by the end, will not only have fallen in love, but they'll have earned that love. They will deserve every happiness they've worked for. Could you imagine picking up a Mystery novel and...never finding out whodunnit? Of course not!<br /><br />In Romancelandia, you have either a Happily Ever After (HEA), or a Happily For Now (HFN). This is the Golden Rule in Romance. They overcome remarkable odds and they win at the end. Someone actually said “Not all books have to have a happy ending...” well, yeah, in Romances, they kinda do. It’s the point of reading a Romance novel, rather than say, a Literary Fiction, or Urban Fantasy. And I’ve seen people mention that the WARDen is leaning towards UF, but I call shenanigans. She’s going back to her roots with <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/23355896.The_Bourbon_Kings__The_Bourbon_Kings___1_" title="The Bourbon Kings (The Bourbon Kings, #1) by J.R. Ward" rel="nofollow noopener">The Bourbon Kings</a> and the Black Dagger Legacy books <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/24903031.Blood_Kiss__Black_Dagger_Legacy___1_" title="Blood Kiss (Black Dagger Legacy, #1) by J.R. Ward" rel="nofollow noopener">Blood Kiss</a>. She obviously knew her fans want more romance, or she wouldn’t be going back to it.<br /><br /><br />And this book wasn’t UF. It was a Romance with no HEA.<br /><br /><br />I’m done with the Brothers, which is a shame since they were my first introduction to vampires post-Twilight. I’m done with Ward, because I don’t trust she won’t do this again to us.<br /><br />Her comment about how she grieved for her dog through this book...then write this, let it be cathartic, then put it away. Write the book with a HEA, and then release the other part as a bonus 6 months down the road. It’s a win all around! And I dno’t think anyone would be mad, because they’d have gotten the HEA. KMM did it with the <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/112755.The_Dark_Highlander__Highlander___5_" title="The Dark Highlander (Highlander, #5) by Karen Marie Moning" rel="nofollow noopener">The Dark Highlander</a> by putting most of her first draft in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/112749.Into_the_Dreaming__Highlander___8_" title="Into the Dreaming (Highlander, #8) by Karen Marie Moning" rel="nofollow noopener">Into the Dreaming</a>, it made a lot of money, and we all had the other version so we were happy.<br /><br /><br />I haven’t even touched on the minor romance where iAm gets his HEA. Maybe maybe if this had been iAm’s book where his romance was forefront, and 500+ pages were dedicated to him, rather than Trez and Selena, I’d be more okay. But his romance is so secondary and so minimal, that it definitely doesn’t take the sting from the betrayal. If anything, I think it makes it worse.<br /><br />Next up is Rhage and Mary. Again. DON’T MESS WITH THEIR HEA, WARD! Why return to them, and give them some contrived issue about his prior promiscuity? Why not move on to Saxton? Or Layla and Xcor? (which btw, WTF, Ward, was that even necessary?).<br /><br /><br />So, I’m done. I’m out. The End. I won’t be returning to the BDB, I won’t be reading Ward’s spin-off, or her new Contemporary series, even as she cries Romance! I have romance again! I can’t. It’s not even a matter of principals, it’s that, as I said, she broke my trust, and I won’t go back for seconds. <br /><br /><b>TL;DR</b><br /><br />This reads like the previous BDB books, but the heroine dies at the end. I won't read Ward again, she's broken my trust as a reader, and pissed me off.</span>
  <a data-text-id="2342278753726540" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_903352977" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/903352977" />
    <a title="❤️ Dorsey aka Wrath Lover Reviews ❤️" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5205999-dorsey-aka-wrath-lover-reviews"><img alt="❤️ Dorsey aka Wrath Lover Reviews ❤️" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1485279859p2/5205999.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/903352977?book_show_action=true">Apr 06, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="❤️ Dorsey aka Wrath Lover Reviews ❤️" class="user" itemprop="url" name="❤️ Dorsey aka Wrath Lover Reviews ❤️" href="/user/show/5205999-dorsey-aka-wrath-lover-reviews">❤️ Dorsey aka Wrath Lover Reviews ❤️</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Audiobook 9781101887851" href="/book/show/40045517-the-shadows">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5205999-dorsey-aka-wrath-lover-reviews?shelf=audio_books">audio_books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5205999-dorsey-aka-wrath-lover-reviews?shelf=jr_ward">jr_ward</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5205999-dorsey-aka-wrath-lover-reviews?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer903352977" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6249859242217874852"><b>
  <i>4.5 Emotionally Battered Stars!!</i>
</b><br/><br/>I laughed, I cried, I laughed some more, than I cried some more, and finally my heart crumbled in pure agony!! This is going to be a difficult review, I don't want to give anything away about the outcome.....<br/><br/><b>Trez and Selena:</b><br/>I've been intrigued by the Shadows since Rhev's book <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/5098079.Lover_Avenged__Black_Dagger_Brotherhood___7_' title='Lover Avenged (Black Dagger Brotherhood, #7) by J.R. Ward' rel='nofollow noopener'>Lover Avenged</a>. I didn't think that the WARDen could pull off Trez being worthy of a Chosen because of his manwhoring ways, he came off as..... I don't know...not callus because he was alw</span>
  <span id="freeText6249859242217874852" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>4.5 Emotionally Battered Stars!!</i>
</b><br><br>I laughed, I cried, I laughed some more, than I cried some more, and finally my heart crumbled in pure agony!! This is going to be a difficult review, I don't want to give anything away about the outcome.....<br><br><b>Trez and Selena:</b><br>I've been intrigued by the Shadows since Rhev's book <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/5098079.Lover_Avenged__Black_Dagger_Brotherhood___7_" title="Lover Avenged (Black Dagger Brotherhood, #7) by J.R. Ward" rel="nofollow noopener">Lover Avenged</a>. I didn't think that the WARDen could pull off Trez being worthy of a Chosen because of his manwhoring ways, he came off as..... I don't know...not callus because he was always respectful to the women he used but still, I couldn't see him with Selena. Now I can't imagine him with anyone else, and I now see him as one of the most honorable men in the series. <br><br>Now for Selena, that Chosen certainly surprised the heck out of me!!!! I didn't expect her to be so vibrant, so fearless, so inspiring, so sexual!! Her enthusiasm for life is off the charts!! She's a fighter, she fought for the man who held her heart and won!! I was totally unprepared and shattered by their story.<br><br><a href="http://s1186.photobucket.com/user/dshewey1/media/Book%20Review%20Photos/PicsArt_1427946521109_zpsuuq1mjci.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1428110082i/14369024.jpg" alt=" photo PicsArt_1427946521109_zpsuuq1mjci.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>iAm and Maichen:</b><br>iAm is kind of brother you would love to have, he is fiercely loyal and protective. He would do anything for Trez. He was there as always at Trez' side knowing the threat of losing Trez to the S'Hisbe. Then when things are intense for him (<i>like really intense</i>) he meets Maichen and it looks as though he has finally, <i>finally</i> found someone. The attraction was unexpected but it seemed doomed from the beginning, Maichen has secrets but feels if she reveals them, she may lose him too soon.<br><br><a href="http://s1186.photobucket.com/user/dshewey1/media/Book%20Review%20Photos/PicsArt_1427947369765_zpsfheos5ge.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1428110377i/14369131.jpg" alt=" photo PicsArt_1427947369765_zpsfheos5ge.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>s'Ex, "The Executioner":</b><br>s'Ex has a pretty big roll in this book as the s'Hisbe leader of the Queen's army and head executioner. He is ruthless, and seems to be unfeeling and sworn to his Queen. However; we see a new side to him, and I came to care about him.<br><br><a href="http://s1186.photobucket.com/user/dshewey1/media/Book%20Review%20Photos/PicsArt_1428111080426_zpscrdt6wq6.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1428111198i/14369292.jpg" alt=" photo PicsArt_1428111080426_zpscrdt6wq6.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>Xcor and Layla:</b><br>We get a couple of revelations regarding Layla's pregnancy and her relationship with Xcor...Layla is so conflicted, I feel for her...I don't know how much longer she can continue with her deceptions to the King, the Brotherhood, and Qhuinn &amp; Blay. Her and Xcor feel deeply for one another and should be together but how? Xcor is responsible for the attempted assisanation and dethroning of (my) Wrath...I don't see good things coming.<br><br><blockquote>
<b><i>“She is....the moon in my night sky”. And that is the beginning, middle, and end of it. There is no more to be told than that, and never shall I speak of her again.</i></b> - Xcor to the BoB on Layla</blockquote><br><br>Now really, who would have thought that such beautiful words can come out of Xcor's mouth!? There was some changes within the Band of Bastards, we'll have to see how this will play out....<br><br><a href="http://s1186.photobucket.com/user/dshewey1/media/Book%20Review%20Photos/PicsArt_1427948517685_zpsbfuwodwp.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1428110453i/14369136.jpg" alt=" photo PicsArt_1427948517685_zpsbfuwodwp.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>Rhage, Mary, and The Brotherhood:</b><br>Rhage was very front &amp; center in this book, I have a feeling on where this storyline will be going in the future but I'll keep those thoughts to myself and keep my fingers crossed that I'm right. The “original” brothers are all part of this book and it was awesome to have them back, not to mention the bantering...<i>loved</i> it!!<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Rhage cleared his throat. “My lord and ruler, Wrath, son of Wrath, blooded father of Wrath, I present you with Throe, Piece of Shit”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><a href="http://s1186.photobucket.com/user/dshewey1/media/BDB/IMG_3617020965571_zpsrtm9drsg.jpeg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1428111488i/14369339.jpg" alt=" photo IMG_3617020965571_zpsrtm9drsg.jpeg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Qhuinn's brother Luchas is still recovering after his rescue from the Lessers, but he has given up on his battered body &amp; soul. While Q does all he can to to get him not to give up on his life.<br><br><blockquote>
<b><i>“I know what it’s like to not have hope,” Qhuinn said roughly. “But destiny can surprise you.”</i></b>- Q to Luchas</blockquote><br><br><b>A little Insight into BDB Legacy:</b><br>We meet and get to know Paradise, the blooded daughter of Abalone, First Adviser to the King who will be featured in the first book <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/25144725.Blood_Kiss__Black_Dagger_Legacy___1_" title="Blood Kiss (Black Dagger Legacy, #1) by J.R. Ward" rel="nofollow noopener">Blood Kiss</a> in the BDB spin-off series <i>
  <b>BDB Legacy</b>
</i>, I really liked her and look forward to getting more of her. Her hero, Craeg was briefly introduced, he seems to be very shy &amp; sweet....<i>I can't wait</i>!!!<br><br><b>My only disappointment:</b><br>I thought it was announced that Murhder would be in this book....I was sooooo looking forward to him coming back to the Brotherhood, which is reflected in my rating (otherwise it would have been a 5 Star rating, such was my disappointment). Was I mistaken or did he appear and it was a snippet so small that I missed it? <br><br>Either way, I loved it but at the same time I hated how some storylines played out, I have to believe that the WARDen knows what she's doing. <br><br><b>4/05/15 Update (Q&amp;A in Cincinnati yesterday)!!!!:<br>I knew I read that Murhder would be in this book!!!!<br><a href="http://s1186.photobucket.com/user/dshewey1/media/Book%20Review%20Photos/IMG_1695_zpsv9p4rpad.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1428218374i/14389810.jpg" alt=" photo IMG_1695_zpsv9p4rpad.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a></b></span>
  <a data-text-id="6249859242217874852" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_985596774" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/985596774" />
    <a title="P " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/25327841-p"><img alt="P " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1489853536p2/25327841.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/985596774?book_show_action=true">Jul 03, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="P " class="user" itemprop="url" name="P " href="/user/show/25327841-p">P </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25327841-p?shelf=paranormal-romance">paranormal-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer985596774" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14333516362197941148"><b>
  <blockquote>“She is . . . the moon in my night sky. And that is the beginning, middle, and end of it. There is no more to be told than that, and never shall I speak of her again.” </blockquote>
</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1481200331i/21397368.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I've been waiting for this book since I finished The King, and consequently my hope was too high before I could get my hands on this beautiful book. The Shadows follows after what happened to Trez and iAm in the previous one, while Trez can't stop whoring himself, iAm is trying to fix things his brother has done until now. The</span>
  <span id="freeText14333516362197941148" style="display:none"><b>
  <blockquote>“She is . . . the moon in my night sky. And that is the beginning, middle, and end of it. There is no more to be told than that, and never shall I speak of her again.” </blockquote>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1481200331i/21397368.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I've been waiting for this book since I finished The King, and consequently my hope was too high before I could get my hands on this beautiful book. The Shadows follows after what happened to Trez and iAm in the previous one, while Trez can't stop whoring himself, iAm is trying to fix things his brother has done until now. The story revolves around Trez and Selena at first, but around the middle, we get to see more of iAm and his actions to help his only brother.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>“Phury Syndrome—a condition whereupon one brother was so fucked-up that the other fell into a black hole trying to save him.”</blockquote>
</b> <br><br>The story of this book is heartbreaking and painful, yet it's so beautiful in the same time. I kept asking myself why I was this happy when I wasn't supposed to feel like that, and finally I've got an answer to my question. Why is this book so exquisite <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ even though the ending is sad and unacceptable for some readers <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> ? Because I know that love shouldn't be taken for granted. Love is precious, of course, but its value only exists for a limited time. What Ward shows us in this book isn't even out of that concept. She did her job very well when she started writing The Shadows because she knew where to start and end it.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>“Rhage cleared his throat. “My lord and ruler, Wrath, son of Wrath, blooded father of Wrath, I present you with Throe, Piece of Shit.”</blockquote>
</b> <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1450280181ra/17404223.gif" width="400" height="230" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This is the book that I can't get it out of my head and my mind even I read it the first time last year. That scene <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[when Trez keeps telling Selena that he loves her repeatedly <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> is very epic and unforgettable. <br><br>I was satisfied by the ending and what follows after. The Shadows was my new experience for reading something different in this genre. I'm glad I picked this one up, it's worth every single drop of my tears. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1481200331ra/21397369.gif" width="400" height="280" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://goo.gl/ERBmiS">https://goo.gl/ERBmiS</a></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="14333516362197941148" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_923480920" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/923480920" />
    <a title="Alisa" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/12256655-alisa"><img alt="Alisa" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1447707844p2/12256655.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/923480920?book_show_action=true">Apr 28, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Alisa" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Alisa" href="/user/show/12256655-alisa">Alisa</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12256655-alisa?shelf=vampires">vampires</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12256655-alisa?shelf=zz-2015">zz-2015</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer923480920" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10683870202008582741"><a href='http://s1318.photobucket.com/user/pinewyz/media/britneyisnotfeelingit_zpsvrbecylx.gif.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1428166846ra/14380079.gif' alt=' photo britneyisnotfeelingit_zpsvrbecylx.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><br/>Britney is not the only one not feeling it. I can not believe how boring this book was. I was as bored as a stone statue (oh yes I did go there). I'm not even going to write a comprehensive review. I'm just going to jump from one rant to another. I mean if the author can write an almost 600 pg book just jumping around randomly from plotline to plotline then why can't I? <b>(There will be spoilers in my rants so stop right now if you don't want to know stuff)</b><br/><br/>1. I loathe these Chosen chicks. Like</span>
  <span id="freeText10683870202008582741" style="display:none"><a href="http://s1318.photobucket.com/user/pinewyz/media/britneyisnotfeelingit_zpsvrbecylx.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1428166846ra/14380079.gif" alt=" photo britneyisnotfeelingit_zpsvrbecylx.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>Britney is not the only one not feeling it. I can not believe how boring this book was. I was as bored as a stone statue (oh yes I did go there). I'm not even going to write a comprehensive review. I'm just going to jump from one rant to another. I mean if the author can write an almost 600 pg book just jumping around randomly from plotline to plotline then why can't I? <b>(There will be spoilers in my rants so stop right now if you don't want to know stuff)</b><br><br>1. I loathe these Chosen chicks. Like really a lot. I think the series has gone down hill since they started being mates. What happened to the strong heroines from the begining of the series? I want more Bellas, Marys and Beths. I'll even take bad assed warrior females like Xhex and Paine. These milk toast Chosen just have to go.<br>This is a quote from Ward's own blog post about the Chosen:<br><br><i>Fast forward a couple of years and a couple more stories, and it was funny, the idea of doing another Chosen falling in love- considering that I'd already done Phury and Cormia- was a total snooze to me. One of the issues with the Chosen is that, as they have been emerging from their cult-like upbringing, there isn't a lot of personality to them. </i><br><br>What on earth? If even you know how boring they are WHY ARE YOU WRITING THE THIRD DARN BOOK ABOUT THEM??(and that's not even counting the endless Layla drama)<br><br>2. WTF on Assail? He and his story took up half of Qhuinn and Blay's book. Seriously....100's of pages. Why? Why take away from their story? What was the flipping point if were going to spend the next two books with only a few glimpses of him doing cocaine? <br><br>3. What the heck happened to Layla? I disliked her immensely the first few books she was in but then she stepped up during Qhuinn's book and showed some back bone. I thought I was going to end up liking her but apparently not. She was ridiculousy stupid in this book. There were a bunch of scenes in this book where I wanted to throat punch her but the one that really made me mad was when she gets so upset seeing Xcor jack off that she trips and falls hard enough to break her arm. Really? You were SO traumatized over a guy holding his penis that you endanger your child/children? How I am supposed to buy in to this nonsense? She didn't get pregnant through immaculate conception. She spent two days letting Qhuinn screw her brains out. I would think she could handle a little jacking off. Stupid. Just stupid. All her whining and sneaking around and playing dumb games with Xcor makes me want throttle her. <br><br>4. The Band of Brothers. Still hate them all. Don't know why we have to have all these scenes with them where absolutely nothing happens. Don't understand why they still speak Old World English. That's a petty complain I know but it's just so stupid to me. They buy clothes, eat out, go to stores, rent houses etc. How can they not know current English? If the Brothers can learn urban slang and speak it to the point you want to beat them then the BOB should be able to speak normally. And on that note... enough with the urban slang. It's ok with V cuz that's always been him but now everyone talks that way. Even Manny and Lassiter. Enough with that. Stop it!<br><br>5. iAm got a shit side story. It could have been good if he would have actually had some time for his story to be told. As it was is was a snooze fest insta love. And let's talk about their first sex scene. I know they were both virgins but couldn't we have gotten more than them kissing and then him pushing his boy part into her girl part? Wow, how romantic. And how they both had fabulous orgasms from that I do not know.<br><br>6. The heroine dies. Really? First of all that's just a bunch of bullshit. You don't kill the heroine in a love story. But I have to be honest and admit I didn't care. That was my biggest problem. I just did not care. How is that possible? I ugly cried in some of the first books. No telling how many Kleenex I went through in Z's book. We know Ward can write emotions like no other yet this storyline was so damn boring that I didn't cry. I didn't get teary-eyed. Nothing. <br><br>7. I'm over all the multiple story lines. It's too much. They're out of control. Too much going on and as a result no one actually gets the time devoted to their stories that they should. <br><br>8. Paradise is boring. I don't care if she goes to the training or not. In fact I don't want to see her again. Another 20 something year old virgin in a book. Yay...we've never seen that before (*gigantic eye roll*) Craeg seemed like he might be interesting but..... Most importantly I don't want to start another series just to get back to the way BDB used to be. How about Ward stop writing all these storylines and go back to one, two things a book? There's plenty of characters who could have a book about them. I refuse to start a new series and pay another $12 for the author to fix the mess that this has turned in to. <br><br>The absolute only things I liked in this book were some of the moments between Rhev and Trez and then Trez and iAm. Some of those were touching. <br><br>There is a REALLY good chance that this the end of my relationship w/Ward and the Brothers. I am definitely not reading the new series and I just don't know about this one. I think I'm done.</span>
  <a data-text-id="10683870202008582741" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>
